Indeed Iraq and its people are a neck stretched toward you, so hasten, hasten (hayta hayta)."

Meaning: come and draw near.

Others recited it "hi'tu laka," with kasra on the ha and the hamza, and damma on the ta, meaning "I have prepared myself for you," from the expression of one who says "hi'tu lil-amri ahi'u hay'atan" (I readied myself for the matter). Among those from whom this recitation was reported are Ibn Abbas, Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Sulami, Abu Wa'il, Ikrimah, and Qatadah, all of whom interpreted it to mean "I have prepared myself for you."

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Amr and al-Kisa'i used to reject this recitation. Abdullah ibn Ishaq recited it "hayti," with fatha on the ha and kasra on the ta, and this is a gharib (rare/singular) recitation.

Others, among them the majority of the people of Madinah, recited it "haytu," with fatha on the ha and damma on the ta, and he cited the poet's words:

"My people are not the most distant, when a caller from the clan says: haytu."

Abd al-Razzaq said: al-Thawri informed us, from al-A'mash, from Abu Wa'il, who said: Ibn Mas'ud said: I have heard the reciters and found them close to one another in their recitations, so recite as you have been taught, and beware of excessive pedantry and disputation, for it is merely like one of you saying "halumma" and "ta'ala" (both meaning "come"). Then Abdullah recited {heyta laka}, and it was said to him: O Abu Abd al-Rahman, some people recite it "haytu laka"? Abdullah said: I recite it as I was taught; that is dearer to me.

Ibn Jarir also said: [chain] Abu Wa'il said: Abdullah recited {heyta laka}, and Masruq said to him: some people recite it "haytu laka"? He said: leave me be, for I recite as I was taught to recite; that is dearer to me.

He also said: [chain] Ibn Mas'ud said: {heyta laka} with fatha on the ha and the ta, and without hamza.

Others recited it "hitu laka," with kasra on the ha, sukun on the ya, and damma on the ta.

Abu Ubaydah Ma'mar ibn al-Muthanna said: "hayta" is not put in the dual, plural, or feminine form; rather, all are addressed with a single form, so one says: "hayta laka" (to a man), "hayta laki" (to a woman), "hayta lakuma" (to two), "hayta lakum" (to a group), and "hayta lahunna" (to women).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ امْرَأَةِ الْعَزِيزِ الَّتِي كَانَ يُوسُفُ فِي بَيْتِهَا بِمِصْرَ، وَقَدْ أَوْصَاهَا زَوْجُهَا بِهِ وَبِإِكْرَامِهِ [ ﴿وَرَاوَدَتْهُ الَّتِي هُوَ فِي بَيْتِهَا] عَنْ نَفْسِهِ﴾ أَيْ: حَاوَلَتْهُ عَلَى نَفْسِهِ، وَدَعَتْهُ إِلَيْهَا، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهَا أَحَبَّتْهُ حُبًّا شَدِيدًا لِجَمَالِهِ وَحُسْنِهِ وَبَهَائِهِ، فَحَمَلَهَا ذَلِكَ عَلَى أَنْ تَجَمَّلَتْ لَهُ، وَغَلَّقَتْ عَلَيْهِ الْأَبْوَابَ، وَدَعَتْهُ إِلَى نَفْسِهَا، ﴿وَقَالَتْ هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ فَامْتَنَعَ مِنْ ذلك أشد الامتناع، و ﴿قَالَ مَعَاذَ اللَّهِ إِنَّهُ رَبِّي [أَحْسَنَ مَثْوَايَ] ﴾ وَكَانُوا يُطْلِقُونَ "اَلرَّبَّ" عَلَى السَّيِّدِ وَالْكَبِيرِ، أَيْ: إِنَّ بَعْلَكِ رَبِّي أَحْسَنَ مَثْوَايَ أَيْ: مَنْزِلِي وَأَحْسَنَ إِلَيَّ، فَلَا أُقَابِلُهُ بِالْفَاحِشَةِ فِي أَهْلِهِ، ﴿إِنَّهُ لَا يُفْلِحُ الظَّالِمُونَ﴾ قَالَ ذَلِكَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَ الْقُرَّاءُ فِي قِرَاءَةِ: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ فَقَرَأَهُ كَثِيرُونَ بِفَتْحِ الْهَاءِ، وَإِسْكَانِ الْيَاءِ، وَفَتْحِ التَّاءِ. وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: مَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّهَا تَدْعُوهُ إِلَى نَفْسِهَا. وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، وَالْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ تَقُولُ: هَلُمَّ لَكَ. وَكَذَا قَالَ زِرّ بْنُ حُبَيْشٍ، وعِكْرِمة، وَالْحَسَنُ وَقَتَادَةُ.

قَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ عبُيَد، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ: وَهِيَ كَلِمَةٌ بِالسُّرْيَانِيَّةِ، أَيْ: عَلَيْكَ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ أَيْ: هَلُمَّ لَكَ، وَهِيَ بِالْقِبْطِيَّةِ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: هِيَ لُغَةٌ عَرَبِيَّةٌ تَدْعُوهُ بِهَا.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ هَلُم لَكَ بالحَوْرَانية.

وَهَكَذَا ذَكَرَهُ مُعَلَّقًا، وَقَدْ أَسْنَدَهُ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سُهَيْل الْوَاسِطِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا قُرَّة بْنُ قيسى، حَدَّثَنَا النَّضْرُ بْنُ عَرَبِيٍّ الجَزَري ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ مَوْلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ قَالَ: هَلُمَّ لَكَ. قَالَ: هِيَ بالْحَوْرَانِيَّةِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ الْقَاسِمُ بْنُ سَلَّامٍ: وَكَانَ الْكِسَائِيُّ يَحْكِي هَذِهِ الْقِرَاءَةَ -يَعْنِي: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ -وَيَقُولُ: هِيَ لُغَةٌ، لِأَهْلِ حَوْران، وَقَعَتْ إِلَى أَهْلِ الْحِجَازِ، مَعْنَاهَا: تَعَالَ. وَقَالَ أَبُو عُبَيْدٍ: سَأْلَتُ شَيْخًا عَالِمًا مِنْ أَهْلِ حَوْرَانَ، فَذَكَرَ أَنَّهَا لغتهم يعرفها.

وَاسْتَشْهَدَ الْإِمَامُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَلَى هَذِهِ الْقِرَاءَةِ بِقَوْلِ الشَّاعِرِ لِعَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ:

أَبْلْغ أَمِيَر المؤمِنين ... أَخا العِراَقِ إذَا أَتَينَا ...

إنَّ العِراقَ وَأَهْلَهُ ... عُنُقٌ إليكَ فَهَيتَ هَيْتا ...

يَقُولُ: فَتَعَالَ وَاقْتَرِبْ 

وَقَرَأَ ذَلِكَ آخَرُونَ: "هِئتُ لَكَ" بِكَسْرِ الْهَاءِ وَالْهَمْزَةِ، وَضَمِّ التَّاءِ، بِمَعْنَى: تَهَيَّأْتُ لَكَ، مِنْ قَوْلِ الْقَائِلِ: هِئْتُ لِلْأَمْرِ أهىِ هيْئَة وَمِمَّنْ رُوِيَ عَنْهُ هَذِهِ الْقِرَاءَةُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَأَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ السُّلَمِيُّ، وَأَبُو وَائِلٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَكُلُّهُمْ يُفَسِّرُهَا بِمَعْنَى: تَهَيَّأْتُ لَكَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَكَانَ أَبُو عَمْرٍو وَالْكِسَائِيُّ يُنْكِرَانِ هَذِهِ الْقِرَاءَةَ. وَقَرَأَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ هَيْتِ"،" بِفَتْحِ الْهَاءِ وَكَسْرِ التَّاءِ: وَهِيَ غَرِيبَةٌ.

وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ، مِنْهُمْ عَامَّةُ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ "هَيْتُ" بِفَتْحِ الْهَاءِ، وَضَمِّ التَّاءِ، وَأَنْشَدَ قَوْلَ الشَّاعِرِ: 

لَيسَ قَومِي بالأبْعَدِين إِذَا مَا ... قَالَ دَاعٍ منَ العَشِيرِةَ: هَيتُ ...

قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَنْبَأَنَا الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي وَائِلٍ قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: قَدْ سَمِعْتُ القَرَأة فَسَمِعْتُهُمْ مُتَقَارِبِينَ، فَاقْرَءُوا كَمَا عُلِّمتم، وَإِيَّاكُمْ وَالتَّنَطُّعَ وَالِاخْتِلَافَ، فَإِنَّمَا هُوَ كَقَوْلِ أَحَدِكُمْ: "هَلُمَّ" وَ"تَعَالَ" ثُمَّ قَرَأَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، إِنَّ نَاسًا يَقْرَءُونَهَا: "هَيْتُ [لَك] " ؟ فَقَالَ عبد الله: إني أقرأها كَمَا عُلِّمت، أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُيَيْنة، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ أَبِي وَائِلٍ قَالَ: قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ فَقَالَ لَهُ مَسْرُوقٌ: إِنَّ نَاسًا يَقْرَءُونَهَا: "هَيْتُ لَك"؟ فَقَالَ: دَعُونِي، فَإِنِّي أَقْرَأُ كَمَا أقْرِئتُ، أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ 

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنِي الْمُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا آدَمُ بْنُ أَبِي إِيَاسٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ شَقِيقٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قال: ﴿هَيْتَ لَكَ﴾ بنصب الهاء والتاء ولا بهمز.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: "هِيْتُ لَك"، بِكَسْرِ الْهَاءِ، وَإِسْكَانِ الْيَاءِ، وَضَمِّ التَّاءِ.

قَالَ أَبُو عُبَيدة مَعْمَرُ بْنُ الْمُثَنَّى: "هَيْتَ" لَا تُثَنَّى وَلَا تُجْمَعُ وَلَا تُؤَنَّثُ، بَلْ يُخَاطَبُ الْجَمِيعُ بِلَفْظٍ وَاحِدٍ، فيقال: هيتَ لَك، وهيتَ لك، ِ وهيتَ لَكُمَا، وهيتَ لَكُمْ، وهيتَ لَهُنَّ

---

## 12:24 — verse 24

### Translation

The statements and expressions of people have differed on this point. What Ibn Jarir and others have mentioned has been narrated from Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and a group of the salaf regarding this matter. And Allah knows best.

Some of them said: what is meant by his inclination toward her is the passing inclination of an inward thought (hadith al-nafs). Al-Baghawi related this from some of the people of verification, then al-Baghawi cited here the hadith of Abd al-Razzaq, from Ma'mar, from Hammam, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah the Exalted says: When My servant intends to do a good deed, write it down for him as one good deed. If he does it, write it down for him as ten times its like. And if he intends to do a bad deed but does not do it, write it down as a good deed, for he only left it for My sake. But if he does it, write it down as its equivalent."

This hadith is recorded in the two Sahihs (Bukhari and Muslim) and has many wordings, this being one of them.

It has also been said: he intended to strike her. And it has been said: he desired her as a wife. And it has been said that {and he inclined toward her had he not seen the proof of his Lord} means: he did not incline toward her at all.

There is a difficulty with this view from the standpoint of the Arabic language, as mentioned by Ibn Jarir and others.

As for the proof (burhan) that he saw, there are also several opinions about it. From Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Muhammad ibn Sirin, al-Hasan, Qatadah, Abu Salih, al-Dahhak, Muhammad ibn Ishaq, and others: he saw the form of his father Ya'qub (peace be upon him) biting his finger with his mouth.

And it has been said of him, in one report: he struck Yusuf in the chest.

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: he saw the phantom of the king, meaning his master. And Muhammad ibn Ishaq said likewise, in what he related from some of them: it was only the phantom of Itfir, his master, when he drew near the door.

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb narrated to us, Waki' narrated to us, from Abu Mawdud, I heard from Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi who said: Yusuf raised his head toward the ceiling of the house, and there was writing on the wall of the house: {And do not approach fornication, indeed it is an indecency and an evil way} [al-Isra: 32].

Abu Ma'shar al-Madani related the same from Muhammad ibn Ka'b.

Abdullah ibn Wahb said: Nafi' ibn Yazid informed me, from Abu Sakhr, who said: I heard al-Qurazi say concerning the "proof" (burhan) that Yusuf saw: three verses from the Book of Allah: {And indeed, over you are keepers} [al-Infitar: 10], and His saying: {And you are not in any matter} [Yunus: 61], and His saying: {Then is He who is a maintainer of every soul, in charge of what it has earned...} [al-Ra'd: 33]. Nafi' said: I heard Abu Hilal say the same as what al-Qurazi said, and he added a fourth verse: {And do not approach fornication} [al-Isra: 32].

Al-Awza'i said: he saw a verse from the Book of Allah on the wall forbidding him from that.

Ibn Jarir said: the correct view is to say that he saw some of the signs of Allah which restrained him from what he had inclined toward. It is possible that it was the form of Ya'qub, and it is possible that it was the form of the king, and it is possible that what he saw was something written that forbade that. There is no decisive proof to specify any particular one of these, so the correct approach is to leave it general, as Allah the Exalted stated it.

He said: and His saying, {Thus, that We might turn away from him evil and immorality} means: just as We showed him a proof that turned him away from what he was engaged in, likewise We protect him from evil and immorality in all his affairs.

{Indeed, he was of Our sincere servants} means: among the chosen, the purified, the selected, the elect, the good ones ﷺ.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

اخْتَلَفَتْ أَقْوَالُ النَّاسِ وَعِبَارَاتُهُمْ فِي هَذَا الْمَقَامِ، وَقَدْ رُوِيَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَطَائِفَةٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ فِي ذَلِكَ مَا ذَكَرَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَغَيْرُهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: الْمُرَادُ بِهَمِّهِ بِهَا هَمّ خَطَرات حَدِيثِ النَّفْسِ. حَكَاهُ الْبَغَوِيُّ عَنْ بَعْضِ أَهْلِ التَّحْقِيقِ، ثُمَّ أَوْرَدَ الْبَغَوِيُّ هَاهُنَا حَدِيثَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَنْ هَمَّامٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: إِذَا هَمّ عَبْدِي بِحَسَنَةٍ فَاكْتُبُوهَا لَهُ حَسَنَةً، فَإِنَّ عَمِلَهَا فَاكْتُبُوهَا لَهُ بِعَشْرِ أَمْثَالِهَا، وَإِنْ هَمَّ بِسَيِّئَةٍ فَلَمْ يَعْمَلْهَا فَاكْتُبُوهَا حَسَنَةً، فَإِنَّمَا تَرَكَهَا مِنْ جَرّائي، فَإِنْ عَمَلِهَا فَاكْتُبُوهَا بِمِثْلِهَا" .

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ مُخَرَّجٌ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ وَلَهُ أَلْفَاظٌ كَثِيرَةٌ، هَذَا مِنْهَا.

وَقِيلَ: هَمَّ بِضَرْبِهَا. وَقِيلَ: تَمَنَّاهَا زَوْجَةً. وَقِيلَ: ﴿وَهَمَّ بِهَا لَوْلا أَنْ رَأَى بُرْهَانَ رَبِّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فَلَمْ يَهِمَّ بِهَا.

وَفِي هَذَا الْقَوْلِ نَظَرٌ مِنْ حَيْثُ الْعَرَبِيَّةِ، ذَكَرَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَغَيْرُهُ .

وَأَمَّا الْبُرْهَانُ الَّذِي رَآهُ فَفِيهِ أَقْوَالٌ أَيْضًا: فَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سِيرِينَ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَقَتَادَةَ، وَأَبِي صَالِحٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ، وَمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، وَغَيْرِهِمْ: رَأَى صُورَةَ أَبِيهِ يَعْقُوبَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَاضًّا عَلَى أُصْبُعِهِ بِفَمِهِ .

وَقِيلَ عَنْهُ فِي رِوَايَةٍ: فَضَرَبَ فِي صَدْرِ يُوسُفَ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: رَأَى خَيَالَ الْمَلِكِ، يَعْنِي: سَيِّدَهُ، وكذا قال محمد بن إسحاق، فِيمَا حَكَاهُ عَنْ بَعْضِهِمْ: إِنَّمَا هُوَ خَيَالُ إِطْفِيرَ سَيِّدِهِ، حِينَ دَنَا مِنَ الْبَابِ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كُرَيْب، حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيعٌ، عَنْ أَبِي مَوْدُودٍ سَمِعْتُ مِنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ القُرَظي قَالَ: رَفَعَ يُوسُفُ رَأْسَهُ إِلَى سَقْفِ الْبَيْتِ، فَإِذَا كِتَابٌ فِي حَائِطِ الْبَيْتِ: ﴿وَلا تَقْرَبُوا الزِّنَا إِنَّهُ كَانَ فَاحِشَةً وَسَاءَ سَبِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٣٢]

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو مَعْشَر الْمَدَنِيُّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي نَافِعُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ، عَنْ أَبِي صَخْرٍ قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ الْقُرَظِيَّ يَقُولُ فِي: "الْبُرْهَانِ" الَّذِي رَأَى يُوسُفُ: ثَلَاثُ آيَاتٍ مِنْ كتاب الله ﴿وَإِنَّ عَلَيْكُمْ لَحَافِظِينَ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الِانْفِطَارِ: ١٠] ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا تَكُونُ فِي شَأْنٍ﴾ الْآيَةَ: [يُونُسَ: ٦١] ، وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَفَمَنْ هُوَ قَائِمٌ عَلَى كُلِّ نَفْسٍ بِمَا كَسَبَتْ﴾ [الرَّعْدِ: ٣٣] قَالَ نَافِعٌ: سَمِعْتُ أَبَا هِلَالٍ يَقُولُ مِثْلَ قَوْلِ الْقُرَظِيِّ، وَزَادَ آيَةً رَابِعَةً ﴿وَلا تَقْرَبُوا الزِّنَا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٣٢]

وَقَالَ الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ: رَأَى آيَةً مِنْ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ فِي الْجِدَارِ تَنْهَاهُ عَنْ ذَلِكَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَالصَّوَابُ أَنْ يُقَالَ: إِنَّهُ رَأَى مِنْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ مَا زَجَرَهُ عَمَّا كَانَ هَمَّ بِهِ، وَجَائِزٌ أَنْ يَكُونَ صُورَةَ يَعْقُوبَ، وَجَائِزٌ أَنْ يَكُونَ [صُورَةَ] الْمَلِكِ، وَجَائِزٌ أَنْ يَكُونَ مَا رَآهُ مَكْتُوبًا مِنَ الزَّجْرِ عَنْ ذَلِكَ. وَلَا حُجَّةَ قَاطِعَةٌ عَلَى تَعْيِينِ شَيْءٍ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، فَالصَّوَابُ أَنْ يُطْلَقَ كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى.

قَالَ: وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ لِنَصْرِفَ عَنْهُ السُّوءَ وَالْفَحْشَاءَ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا أَرَيْنَاهُ بُرْهَانًا صَرَفَهُ عَمَّا كَانَ فِيهِ، كَذَلِكَ نَقِيهِ السُّوءَ وَالْفَحْشَاءَ فِي جَمِيعِ أُمُورِهِ.

﴿إِنَّهُ مِنْ عِبَادِنَا الْمُخْلَصِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْمُجْتَبِينَ الْمُطَهَّرِينَ الْمُخْتَارِينَ الْمُصْطَفَيْنَ الْأَخْيَارِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ.

---

## 12:25-29 — verses 25-29 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs about the state of the two of them when they went out racing toward the door, Yusuf fleeing, and the woman seeking him so that he would return to the house. She caught up with him in the midst of that, and seized his shirt [from behind him], tearing it a dreadful tear. It is said that it fell off him, and Yusuf continued fleeing, going on, while she was in pursuit of him. Then the two of them found her master, who was her husband, at the door. At that point, she extricated herself from the situation she was in through her scheming and cunning, and said to her husband, exonerating herself and casting her own crime upon Yusuf: {What is the recompense of one who intended evil against your wife} that is, a shameful act, {except that he be imprisoned} that is, confined, {or a painful punishment} that is, that he be beaten with a severe, painful beating.

At that point Yusuf, peace be upon him, was vindicated by the truth, and cleared himself of the treachery she had accused him of, saying, righteous and truthful: {It was she who sought to seduce me} And he related that she had pursued him, pulling him toward herself, until she tore his shirt. {And a witness from her household testified: If his shirt is torn from the front,} that is, from in front of him, {then she has spoken truly,} that is, in her statement that he had sought her against her will, because it would then be that when he called her and she refused him, she pushed him away by his chest, and so his shirt was torn, and what she said would be confirmed to be true. {But if his shirt is torn from behind, then she has lied, and he is of the truthful.} And that is what happened, when he fled from her and she pursued him, seizing his shirt from behind him to pull him back to her, and so his shirt was torn from behind him.

They have differed concerning this witness: whether he was a small child or a grown man, there being two opinions among the scholars of the early generations. Abd al-Razzaq said:

[chain] Isra'il, from Simak, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {And a witness from her household testified}: he said, one with a beard.

Al-Thawri said, from Jabir, from Ibn Abi Mulaykah, from Ibn Abbas: he was among the king's close retinue. And likewise said Mujahid, Ikrimah, al-Hasan, Qatadah, al-Suddi, and Muhammad ibn Ishaq: that he was a grown man.

Zayd ibn Aslam and al-Suddi said: he was her cousin.

Ibn Abbas said: he was among the king's close retinue.

Ibn Ishaq mentioned that Zulaykha was the daughter of the sister of the king al-Rayyan ibn al-Walid.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying {And a witness from her household testified}: he said, he was an infant in the cradle. And likewise it has been related from Abu Hurayrah, Hilal ibn Yasaf, al-Hasan, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and al-Dahhak ibn Muzahim: that he was a child in the house. Ibn Jarir preferred this view.

A raised (marfu') hadith has come regarding this. Ibn Jarir said: [chain] al-Hasan ibn Muhammad, from Affan, from Hammad, that is Ibn Salamah, told me Ata' ibn al-Sa'ib, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Four spoke while they were infants," and among them he mentioned the witness of Yusuf.

Another narrated it from Hammad ibn Salamah, from Ata', from Sa'id, from Ibn Abbas, that he said: four spoke while they were infants: the son of Pharaoh's hairdresser, the witness of Yusuf, the companion of Jurayj, and Isa the son of Maryam.

Layth ibn Abi Sulaym said, from Mujahid: he was from the command of Allah, and was not a human being. This is a gharib (singular, unusual) view.

His saying: {But when he saw his shirt torn from behind} that is, when her husband ascertained the truthfulness of Yusuf and the falsehood of what she had accused and cast upon him, {he said, Indeed, this is from your scheming} that is, this slander and defamation with which you have besmirched the honor of this young man is part of your scheming as women, {indeed your scheming is great.}

Then he said, commanding Yusuf, peace be upon him, to conceal what had occurred: O {Yusuf, disregard this} that is, turn away from this matter and pardon it, and do not mention it to anyone, {and ask forgiveness for your sin,} he says to his wife, and he was gentle of temperament and easygoing, or else he excused her because she had seen something she could not restrain herself from. So he said to her: {and ask forgiveness for your sin,} that is, for what occurred from you in intending evil against this young man, then accusing him of that from which he is innocent. Seek forgiveness for what occurred from you, {indeed you have been among the sinners.}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ حَالِهِمَا حِينَ خَرَجَا يَسْتَبِقَانِ إِلَى الْبَابِ، يُوسُفُ هَارِبٌ، وَالْمَرْأَةُ تَطْلُبُهُ لِيَرْجِعَ إِلَى الْبَيْتِ، فَلَحِقَتْهُ فِي أَثْنَاءِ ذَلِكَ، فَأَمْسَكَتْ بِقَمِيصِهِ [مِنْ وَرَائِهِ] فَقَدَّته قَدًّا فَظِيعًا، يُقَالُ: إِنَّهُ سَقَطَ عَنْهُ، وَاسْتَمَرَّ يُوسُفُ هَارِبًا ذَاهِبًا، وَهِيَ فِي إِثْرِهِ، فَأَلْفَيَا سَيِّدَهَا -وَهُوَ زَوْجُهَا -عِنْدَ الْبَابِ، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ خَرَجَتْ مِمَّا هِيَ فِيهِ بِمَكْرِهَا وَكَيْدِهَا، وَقَالَتْ لِزَوْجِهَا مُتَنَصِّلَةً وَقَاذِفَةً يُوسُفَ بَدَائَهَا: ﴿مَا جَزَاءُ مَنْ أَرَادَ بِأَهْلِكَ سُوءًا﴾ أَيْ: فَاحِشَةً، ﴿إِلا أَنْ يُسْجَنَ﴾ أَيْ: يُحْبَسَ، ﴿أَوْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: يُضْرَبَ ضَرْبًا شَدِيدًا مُوجِعًا. فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ انْتَصَرَ يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِالْحَقِّ، وَتَبْرَّأَ مِمَّا رَمَتْهُ بِهِ مِنَ الْخِيَانَةِ، وَقَالَ بَارًّا صَادِقًا ﴿هِيَ رَاوَدَتْنِي عَنْ نَفْسِي﴾ وَذَكَرَ أَنَّهَا اتَّبَعَتْهُ تَجْذِبُهُ إِلَيْهَا حَتَّى قَدَّتْ قَمِيصَهُ، ﴿وَشَهِدَ شَاهِدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِهَا إِنْ كَانَ قَمِيصُهُ قُدَّ مِنْ قُبُلٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ قُدَّامِهِ، ﴿فَصَدَقَتْ﴾ أَيْ: فِي قَوْلِهَا إِنَّهُ أَرَادَهَا عَلَى نَفْسِهَا، لِأَنَّهُ يَكُونُ لَمَّا دَعَاهَا وَأَبَتْ عَلَيْهِ دَفَعَتْهُ فِي صَدْرِهِ، فَقَدَّتْ قَمِيصَهُ، فَيَصِحُّ مَا قَالَتْ: ﴿وَإِنْ كَانَ قَمِيصُهُ قُدَّ مِنْ دُبُرٍ فَكَذَبَتْ وَهُوَ مِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ وَذَلِكَ يَكُونُ كَمَا وَقَعَ لَمَّا هَرَبَ مِنْهَا، وَتَطَلَّبَتْهُ أَمْسَكَتْ بِقَمِيصِهِ مِنْ وَرَائِهِ لِتَرُدَّهُ إِلَيْهَا، فَقَدَّتْ قَمِيصَهُ مِنْ وَرَائِهِ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفُوا فِي هَذَا الشَّاهِدِ: هَلْ هُوَ صَغِيرٌ أَوْ كَبِيرٌ، عَلَى قَوْلَيْنِ لِعُلَمَاءِ السَّلَفِ، فَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ:

أَخْبَرْنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ سِمَاك، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَشَهِدَ شَاهِدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِهَا﴾ قَالَ: ذُو لِحْيَةٍ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي مُلَيْكَة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ مِنْ خَاصَّةِ الْمَلِكِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعِكْرِمَةُ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، والسُّدِّي، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: إِنَّهُ كَانَ رَجُلًا.

وَقَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ: كَانَ ابْنَ عَمِّهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ مِنْ خَاصَّةِ الْمَلِكِ.

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ أَنَّ زُلَيْخَا كَانَتْ بِنْتَ أُخْتِ الْمَلِكِ الرَّيَّانِ بْنِ الْوَلِيدِ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَشَهِدَ شَاهِدٌ مِنْ أَهْلِهَا﴾ قَالَ: كَانَ صَبِيًّا فِي الْمَهْدِ. وَكَذَا رُوي عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، وَهِلَالِ بْنِ يَسَاف، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ وَالضَّحَّاكِ بْنِ مُزاحم: أَنَّهُ كَانَ صَبِيًّا فِي الدَّارِ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِيهِ حَدِيثٌ مَرْفُوعٌ فَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادٌ -هُوَ ابْنُ سَلَمَةَ -أَخْبَرَنِي عَطَاءُ بْنُ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ سعيد بن جبير، عن ابن عباس، عن النبي ﷺ قَالَ: "تَكَلَّمَ أَرْبَعَةٌ وَهُمْ صِغَارٌ"، فَذَكَرَ فِيهِمْ شَاهِدَ يُوسُفَ .

وَرَوَاهُ غَيْرُهُ عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: تَكَلَّمَ أَرْبَعَةٌ وَهُمْ صِغَارٌ: ابْنُ مَاشِطَةِ بِنْتِ فِرْعَوْنَ، وَشَاهِدُ يُوسُفَ، وَصَاحِبُ جُرَيْج، وَعِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ .

وَقَالَ لَيْثُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: كَانَ مِنْ أَمْرِ اللَّهِ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ إِنْسِيًّا. وَهَذَا قَوْلٌ غَرِيبٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَلَمَّا رَأَى قَمِيصَهُ قُدَّ مِنْ دُبُرٍ﴾ أَيْ: فَلَمَّا تَحَقَّقَ زَوْجُهَا صدقَ يُوسُفَ وَكَذِبَهَا فِيمَا قَذَفَتْهُ وَرَمَتْهُ بِهِ، ﴿قَالَ إِنَّهُ مِنْ كَيْدِكُنَّ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ هَذَا الْبُهْتَ واللَّطخ الَّذِي لَطَّخْتِ عِرْضَ هَذَا الشَّابِّ بِهِ مِنْ جُمْلَةِ كَيْدِكُنَّ، ﴿إِنَّ كَيْدَكُنَّ عَظِيمٌ﴾

ثُمَّ قَالَ آمِرًا لِيُوسُفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِكِتْمَانِ مَا وَقَعَ: يَا ﴿يُوسُفُ أَعْرِضْ عَنْ هَذَا﴾ أَيِ: اضْرِبْ عَنْ هَذَا [الْأَمْرِ] صَفْحًا، فَلَا تَذْكُرْهُ لِأَحَدٍ، ﴿وَاسْتَغْفِرِي لِذَنْبِكِ﴾ يَقُولُ لِاِمْرَأَتِهِ وَقَدْ كَانَ لَيِّنَ الْعَرِيكَةِ سَهْلًا أَوْ أَنَّهُ عَذَرَهَا؛ لِأَنَّهَا رَأَتْ مَا لَا صَبْرَ لَهَا عَنْهُ، فَقَالَ لَهَا: ﴿وَاسْتَغْفِرِي لِذَنْبِكِ﴾ أَيِ: الَّذِي وَقَعَ مِنْكِ مِنْ إِرَادَةِ السُّوءِ بِهَذَا الشَّابِّ، ثُمَّ قَذْفه بِمَا هُوَ بَرِيءٌ مِنْهُ، اسْتَغْفِرِي مِنْ هَذَا الَّذِي وَقَعَ مِنْكِ، ﴿إِنَّكِ كُنْتِ مِنَ الْخَاطِئِينَ﴾

---

## 12:30-34 — verses 30-34 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He Most High informs that the news of Yusuf and the wife of the 'Aziz spread throughout the city, which is Egypt, until the people were talking about it. {And women in the city said}, meaning like the wives of the commanders and the notables, condemning the wife of the 'Aziz, who was the minister, and finding fault with her over that: {The wife of the 'Aziz is seeking to seduce her young man against his will}, meaning she is trying to entice her servant away from his self-restraint and calling him to herself. {He has indeed smitten her heart with love (shaghafaha hubban)}, meaning his love had reached the shaghaf of her heart, which is its covering.

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn 'Abbas: al-shaghaf is love that kills, while al-shaghaf (with a different vowel pattern) is less than that, and al-shighaf is the membrane covering the heart.

{Indeed we see her in manifest error}, meaning in this deed of hers, in her love for her young man and her attempt to seduce him against his will.

{So when she heard of their scheming (bi-makrihinna)}, some of them said: meaning their talk. Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: rather, news of Yusuf's beauty reached them, and they wished to see him, so they said what they said in order to find a way to see him and behold him. At that, {she sent for them}, meaning she invited them to her house to host them, {and she prepared for them a banquet (muttaka')}.

Ibn 'Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Mujahid, al-Hasan, al-Suddi, and others said: it was a prepared gathering, containing spreads, cushions, and food, among which was something to be cut with knives, such as citron (utrujj) and the like. Hence He Most High said: {and she gave each one of them a knife}. This was a scheme of hers, matching their own scheming to see him. {And she said, "Come out before them"}, for she had hidden him in another place. {So when} he came out and {they saw him, they exalted him}, meaning they were struck by the greatness of his standing and the magnitude of his worth, and they began to cut their hands in astonishment at the sight of him, thinking they were cutting the citron with the knives. What is meant is that they gashed their hands with them, as more than one has said.

It is reported from Mujahid and Qatadah: they cut their hands until they dropped them, but God knows best.

It is mentioned from Zayd ibn Aslam that she said to them, after they had eaten and their spirits were at ease, then she placed before them citron and gave each one of them a knife: "Would you like to look at Yusuf?" They said: "Yes." So she sent for him, commanding him to come out to them. When they saw him, they began to cut their hands. Then she commanded him to go back, so he went back, so that they might see him coming and going, while they gashed their hands. When they felt the pain they began to wail. She said: "You, from a single glance, have done this, so how can I be blamed?" They said: "God forbid, this is not a human being, this is nothing but a noble angel." Then they said to her: "We do not see any blame upon you after what we have seen," for they had never seen among human beings anyone resembling him or even close to him. For he, blessings and peace of God be upon him, had been given half of all beauty, as is established in the sound hadith concerning the account of the Night Journey: that the Messenger of God ﷺ passed by Yusuf (peace be upon him) in the third heaven, and said: "There he was, having been given half of all beauty."

Hammad ibn Salamah said, from Thabit, from Anas, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Yusuf and his mother were given half of all beauty." Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Abu Ishaq, from Abu al-Ahwas, from 'Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, who said: Yusuf and his mother were given a third of all beauty.

Abu Ishaq also said, from Abu al-Ahwas, from 'Abdullah, who said: Yusuf's face was like lightning, and whenever the woman came to him on some matter, he would cover his face for fear that she would be tempted by him.

Al-Hasan al-Basri also reported it, as a mursal (chain missing a Companion) report from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "Yusuf and his mother were given a third of the beauty of the people of this world, and the rest of mankind were given two-thirds," or he said: "Yusuf and his mother were given two-thirds and mankind was given a third."

Sufyan said, from Mansur, from Mujahid, from Rabi'ah al-Jurashi, who said: beauty was divided into two halves, and Yusuf and his mother Sarah were given half of all beauty, while the other half was distributed among the rest of creation.

The Imam Abu al-Qasim al-Suhayli said: its meaning is that Yusuf possessed half of the beauty of Adam (peace be upon him), for God created Adam with His own hand in the most perfect and beautiful form, and none among his descendants ever equaled him in beauty, and Yusuf was given half of his beauty.

Hence these women said upon seeing him: {God forbid (hasha lillah)}. Mujahid and more than one other said: it means "God forbid" (ma'adh Allah). {This is not a human being}. Some of them read it as "ma hadha bi-shira" meaning "this is not something purchasable."

{This is nothing but a noble angel. She said, "That is the one about whom you blamed me"}, meaning she said this, excusing herself to them, since he was truly worthy of being loved for his beauty and perfection.

{And I certainly sought to seduce him, but he was firmly resistant (fasta'sama)}, meaning he refused. Some of them said: when they saw his outward beauty, she informed them of his fine qualities that were hidden from them, namely chastity along with this beauty. Then she said, threatening: {And if he does not do what I order him, he will surely be imprisoned and will surely be among the humiliated}. At that, Yusuf (peace be upon him) sought refuge from their evil and their scheming, and said: {My Lord, prison is more beloved to me than what they call me to}, meaning than the immorality they were calling him to. {And unless You turn away their scheming from me, I might incline toward them}, meaning: if You leave me to myself, I have no power over myself, nor do I possess for it any harm or benefit except through Your might and Your strength. You are the one from whom help is sought, and upon You is reliance placed, so do not leave me to myself.

{I might incline toward them and be among the ignorant. So his Lord answered him and turned away from him their scheming. Indeed He is the Hearing, the Knowing}. This was because Yusuf (peace be upon him) was protected by God with tremendous protection, and He shielded him, so he refused her most firmly and chose prison over that. This is the utmost of the stations of perfection: that despite his youth, his beauty, and his perfection, his mistress, who was the wife of the 'Aziz of Egypt, called him to herself, and she besides that was at the utmost of beauty, wealth, and rank, yet he refused that and chose prison over it, out of fear of God and hope for His reward.

Hence it is established in the two Sahihs that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "Seven whom God will shade with His shade on the day when there is no shade but His shade: a just ruler; a young man who grew up in the worship of God; a man whose heart is attached to the mosque, from the time he leaves it until he returns to it; two men who loved one another for the sake of God, meeting upon that and parting upon that; a man who gives charity and conceals it, such that his left hand does not know what his right hand has spent; a man who remembers God in private and his eyes overflow with tears; and a man called by a woman of beauty and rank, who says, 'I fear God.'"

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّ خَبَرَ يُوسُفَ وَاِمْرَأَةِ الْعَزِيزِ شَاعَ فِي الْمَدِينَةِ، وَهِيَ مِصْرُ، حَتَّى تَحَدَّثَ النَّاسُ بِهِ، ﴿وَقَالَ نِسْوَةٌ فِي الْمَدِينَةِ﴾ مِثْلُ نِسَاءِ الْأُمَرَاءِ [و] الْكُبَرَاءِ، يُنْكِرْنَ عَلَى امْرَأَةِ الْعَزِيزِ، وَهُوَ الْوَزِيرُ، وَيَعِبْنَ ذَلِكَ عَلَيْهَا: ﴿امْرَأَةُ الْعَزِيزِ تُرَاوِدُ فَتَاهَا عَنْ نَفْسِهِ﴾ أَيْ: تحاول غلامها عن نفسه، وتدعوه إلى نَفْسِهَا، ﴿قَدْ شَغَفَهَا حُبًّا﴾ أَيْ قَدْ: وَصَلَ حُبُّهُ إِلَى شَغَافِ قَلْبِهَا. وَهُوَ غِلَافُهُ.

قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الشَّغَف: الْحُبُّ الْقَاتِلُ، والشَّغَف دُونَ ذَلِكَ، وَالشَّغَافُ: حِجَابُ الْقَلْبِ.

﴿إِنَّا لَنَرَاهَا فِي ضَلالٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ أَيْ: فِي صَنِيعِهَا هَذَا مِنْ حُبِّهَا فَتَاهَا، وَمُرَاوَدَتِهَا إِيَّاهُ عَنْ نَفْسِهِ.

﴿فَلَمَّا سَمِعَتْ بِمَكْرِهِنَّ﴾ قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: بِقَوْلِهِنَّ. وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: بَلْ بَلَغهُنَّ حُسْنُ يُوسُفَ، فَأَحْبَبْنَ أَنْ يَرَيْنَهُ، فَقُلْنَ ذَلِكَ لِيَتَوَصَّلْنَ إِلَى رُؤْيَتِهِ وَمُشَاهَدَتِهِ، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ ﴿أَرْسَلَتْ إِلَيْهِنَّ﴾ أَيْ: دَعَتْهُنَّ إِلَى مَنْزِلِهَا لِتُضَيِّفَهُنَّ ﴿وَأَعْتَدَتْ لَهُنَّ مُتَّكَأً﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ: هُوَ الْمَجْلِسُ الْمُعَدُّ، فِيهِ مَفَارِشُ وَمَخَادُّ وَطَعَامٌ، فِيهِ مَا يُقْطَعُ بِالسَّكَاكِينِ مَنْ أُتْرُجٍّ وَنَحْوِهِ. وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَآتَتْ كُلَّ وَاحِدَةٍ مِنْهُنَّ سِكِّينًا﴾ وَكَانَ هَذَا مَكِيدَةً مِنْهَا، وَمُقَابَلَةً لَهُنَّ فِي احْتِيَالِهِنَّ عَلَى رُؤْيَتِهِ، ﴿وَقَالَتِ اخْرُجْ عَلَيْهِنَّ﴾ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ قَدْ خَبَّأَتْهُ فِي مَكَانٍ آخَرَ، ﴿فَلَمَّا﴾ خَرَجَ وَ ﴿رَأَيْنَهُ أَكْبَرْنَهُ﴾ أَيْ: أَعَظَمْنَ شَأْنَهُ، وَأَجْلَلْنَ قَدْرَهُ؛ وَجَعَلْنَ يُقَطِّعْنَ أَيْدِيَهُنَّ دَهَشا بِرُؤْيَتِهِ، وَهُنَّ يَظْنُنَّ أَنَّهُنَّ يُقَطِّعْنَ الْأُتْرُجَّ بِالسَّكَاكِينِ، وَالْمُرَادُ: أَنَّهُنَّ حَزَّزْنَ أَيْدِيَهُنَّ بِهَا، قَالَهُ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ.

وَعَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَقَتَادَةَ: قَطَّعْنَ أَيْدِيَهُنَّ حَتَّى أَلْقَيْنَهَا، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ ذُكِرَ عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ أنها قالت لهن بعدما أَكَلْنَ وَطَابَتْ أَنْفُسُهُنَّ، ثُمَّ وَضَعَتْ بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِنَّ أُتْرُجًّا وَآتَتْ كُلَّ وَاحِدَةٍ مِنْهُنَّ سِكِّينًا: هَلْ لَكُنَّ فِي النَّظَرِ إِلَى يُوسُفَ؟ قُلْنَ: نَعَمْ. فَبَعَثَتْ إِلَيْهِ تَأْمُرُهُ أَنِ اخْرُجْ إِلَيْهِنَّ فَلَمَّا رَأَيْنَهُ جَعَلْنَ يَقْطَعْنَ أَيْدِيَهُنَّ، ثُمَّ أَمَرَتْهُ أَنْ يَرْجِعَ فَرَجَعَ لِيَرَيْنَهُ مُقْبِلًا وَمُدْبِرًا، وَهُنَّ يُحَزُّزْنَ فِي أَيْدِيهِنَّ، فَلَمَّا أَحْسَسْنَ بِالْأَلَمِ جَعَلْنَ يُوَلْوِلْنَ، فَقَالَتْ: أَنْتُنَّ مِنْ نَظْرَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ فَعَلْتُنَّ هَكَذَا، فَكَيْفَ أُلَامُ أَنَا؟ فَقُلْنَ حَاشَ لِلَّهِ مَا هَذَا بَشَرًا إِنْ هَذَا إِلَّا مَلَكٌ كَرِيمٌ، ثُمَّ قُلْنَ لَهَا: وَمَا نَرَى عَلَيْكِ مِنْ لَوْمٍ بَعْدَ الَّذِي رَأَيْنَا، لِأَنَّهُنَّ لَمْ يَرَيْنَ فِي الْبَشَرِ شَبَهَهُ وَلَا قَرِيبًا مِنْهُ، فَإِنَّهُ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَّمَ كَانَ قَدْ أُعْطِي شَطْرَ الْحُسْنِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ ذَلِكَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الصَّحِيحِ فِي حَدِيثِ الْإِسْرَاءِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ مَرَّ بِيُوسُفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فِي السَّمَاءِ الثَّالِثَةِ، قَالَ: "فَإِذَا هُوَ قَدْ أُعْطِيَ شَطْرَ الْحُسْنِ" 

وَقَالَ حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ ثَابِتٍ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُعْطِيَ يوسف وأمه شطر الْحُسْنِ" وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: أُعْطِيَ يُوسُفُ وَأُمُّهُ ثُلُثَ الْحُسْنِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو إِسْحَاقَ أَيْضًا، عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: كَانَ وَجْهُ يُوسُفَ مَثَلَ الْبَرْقِ، وَكَانَتِ الْمَرْأَةُ إِذَا أَتَتْهُ لِحَاجَةٍ غَطَّى وَجْهَهُ مَخَافَةَ أَنْ تَفْتَتِنَ بِهِ.

وَرَوَاهُ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ مُرْسَلًا عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "أُعْطِيَ يُوسُفُ وَأُمُّهُ ثُلُثَ حُسْنِ أَهْلِ الدُّنْيَا، وَأُعْطِيَ النَّاسُ الثُّلُثَيْنِ -أَوْ قَالَ: أُعْطِيَ يُوسُفُ وَأُمُّهُ الثُّلُثَيْنِ وَالنَّاسُ الثُّلُثَ" 

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ عَنْ رَبِيعَةَ الجُرَشي قَالَ: قُسِمَ الْحُسْنُ نِصْفَيْنِ، فَأُعْطِيَ يُوسُفُ وَأُمُّهُ سَارَّةُ نِصْفَ الْحُسْنِ. وَالنِّصْفُ الْآخَرُ بَيْنَ سَائِرِ الْخَلْقِ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ السُّهَيْلِيُّ: مَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّ يُوسُفَ كَانَ عَلَى النِّصْفِ مِنْ حُسْنِ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ خَلَقَ آدَمَ بِيَدِهِ عَلَى أَكْمَلِ صُورَةٍ وَأَحْسَنِهَا، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ فِي ذُرِّيَّتِهِ مَنْ يُوَازِيهِ فِي جَمَالِهِ، وَكَانَ يُوسُفُ قَدْ أُعْطِيَ شَطْرَ حُسْنِهِ.

فَلِهَذَا قَالَ هَؤُلَاءِ النِّسْوَةُ عِنْدَ رُؤْيَتِهِ: ﴿حَاشَ لِلَّهِ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: مَعَاذَ اللَّهِ، ﴿مَا هَذَا بَشَرًا﴾ وَقَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ: "مَا هَذَا بِشِرىً" أَيْ: بِمُشْتَرًى.

﴿إِنْ هَذَا إِلا مَلَكٌ كَرِيمٌ قَالَتْ فَذَلِكُنَّ الَّذِي لُمْتُنَّنِي فِيهِ﴾ تَقُولُ هَذَا مُعْتَذِرَةً إِلَيْهِنَّ بِأَنَّ هَذَا حَقِيقٌ بِأَنْ يُحَبَّ لِجَمَالِهِ وَكَمَالِهِ.

﴿وَلَقَدْ رَاوَدْتُهُ عَنْ نَفْسِهِ فَاسْتَعْصَمَ﴾ أَيْ: فَامْتَنَعَ. قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: لَمَّا رَأَيْنَ جَمَالَهُ الظَّاهِرَ، أَخْبَرَتْهُنَّ بِصِفَاتِهِ الْحَسَنَةِ الَّتِي تَخْفَى عَنْهُنَّ، وَهِيَ الْعِفَّةُ مَعَ هَذَا الْجَمَالِ، ثُمَّ قَالَتْ تَتَوَعَّدُ ﴿وَلَئِنْ لَمْ يَفْعَلْ مَا آمُرُهُ لَيُسْجَنَنَّ وَلَيَكُونَنْ مِنَ الصَّاغِرِينَ﴾ فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ اسْتَعَاذَ يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مِنْ شَرِّهِنَّ وَكَيْدِهِنَّ، وَقَالَ: ﴿رَبِّ السِّجْنُ أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِمَّا يَدْعُونَنِي إِلَيْهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْفَاحِشَةِ، ﴿وَإِلا تَصْرِفْ عَنِّي كَيْدَهُنَّ أَصْبُ إِلَيْهِنَّ﴾ أَيْ: إِنْ وَكَّلْتَنِي إِلَى نَفْسِي، فَلَيْسَ لِي مِنْ نَفْسِي قُدْرَةٌ، وَلَا أَمَلِكُ لَهَا ضُرًّا وَلَا نَفْعًا إِلَّا بِحَوْلِكَ وَقُوَّتِكَ، أَنْتَ الْمُسْتَعَانُ وَعَلَيْكَ التُّكْلَانُ، فَلَا تَكِلْنِي إِلَى نَفْسِي.

﴿أَصْبُ إِلَيْهِنَّ وَأَكُنْ مِنَ الْجَاهِلِينَ فَاسْتَجَابَ لَهُ رَبُّهُ فَصَرَفَ عَنْهُ كَيْدَهُنَّ إِنَّهُ هُوَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ﴾ وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ يُوسُفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، عَصَمه اللَّهُ عِصْمَةً عَظِيمَةً، وَحَمَاهُ فَامْتَنَعَ منها أشد الامتناع، واختار السجن عَلَى ذَلِكَ، وَهَذَا فِي غَايَةِ مَقَامَاتِ الْكَمَالِ: أَنَّهُ مَعَ شَبَابِهِ وَجَمَالِهِ وَكَمَالِهِ تَدْعُوهُ سَيِّدَتُهُ، وَهِيَ امْرَأَةُ عَزِيزِ مِصْرَ، وَهِيَ مَعَ هَذَا فِي غَايَةِ الْجَمَالِ وَالْمَالِ، وَالرِّيَاسَةِ وَيَمْتَنِعُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ، وَيَخْتَارُ السِّجْنَ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، خَوْفًا مِنَ اللَّهِ وَرَجَاءَ ثَوَابِهِ.

وَلِهَذَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم قَالَ: "سَبْعَةٌ يُظِلُّهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي ظِلِّهِ يَوْمَ لَا ظِلَّ إِلَّا ظِلُّهُ: إِمَامٌ عَادِلٌ، وَشَابٌّ نَشَأَ فِي عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَرَجُلٌ قَلْبُهُ مُعَلَّقٌ بِالْمَسْجِدِ إِذَا خَرَجَ مِنْهُ حَتَّى يَعُودَ إِلَيْهِ، وَرَجُلَانِ تَحَابَّا فِي اللَّهِ اجْتَمَعَا عَلَيْهِ وَافْتَرَقَا عَلَيْهِ، وَرَجُلٌ تَصَدَّقُ بِصَدَقَةٍ فَأَخْفَاهَا حَتَّى لَا تَعْلَمَ شِمَالُهُ مَا أَنْفَقَتْ يَمِينُهُ، وَرَجُلٌ ذَكَرَ اللَّهَ خَالِيًا فَفَاضَتْ عَيْنَاهُ، وَرَجُلٌ دَعَتْهُ امْرَأَةٌ ذَاتُ جَمَالٍ وَمَنْصِبٍ، فَقَالَ: إِنِّي أَخَافُ اللَّهَ"

---

## 12:35 — verse 35

### Translation

He, Exalted, says: then it appeared to them, in what they judged expedient, that they should imprison him for a time, that is, for a period, and this was after they had recognized his innocence and the signs, that is, the proofs, of his truthfulness in his chastity and integrity had become clear. It is as though, and Allah knows best, they only imprisoned him because the story had spread giving the impression that he had solicited her, and that they imprisoned him on that account. This is why, when the great king asked for him at the end of the period, he refused to come out until his innocence of the treachery attributed to him had become manifest. When that was established, he came out with his honor unblemished, the prayers and peace of Allah be upon him.

Al-Suddi mentioned that they only imprisoned him so that what had happened on her part regarding him would not spread, and so that his honor would be cleared, which would have exposed her.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: ثُمَّ ظَهَرَ لَهُمْ مِنَ الْمَصْلَحَةِ فِيمَا رَأَوْهُ أَنَّهُمْ يَسْجُنُونَهُ إِلَى حِينٍ، أَيْ: إِلَى مُدَّةٍ، وَذَلِكَ بعدما عَرَفُوا بَرَاءَتَهُ، وَظَهَرَتِ الْآيَاتُ -وَهِيَ الْأَدِلَّةُ -عَلَى صِدْقِهِ فِي عِفَّتِهِ وَنَزَاهَتِهِ. فَكَأَنَّهُمْ -وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ -إِنَّمَا سَجَنُوهُ لَمَّا شَاعَ الْحَدِيثُ إِيهَامًا أَنَّ هَذَا رَاوَدَهَا عَنْ نَفْسِهَا، وَأَنَّهُمْ سَجَنُوهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ. وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا طَلَبَهُ الْمَلِكُ الْكَبِيرُ فِي آخِرِ الْمُدَّةِ، امْتَنَعَ مِنَ الْخُرُوجِ حَتَّى تَتَبَيَّنَ بَرَاءَتُهُ مِمَّا نُسِبَ إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْخِيَانَةِ، فَلَمَّا تَقَرَّرَ ذَلِكَ خَرَجَ وَهُوَ نَقِيّ الْعِرْضِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَامُهُ.

وَذَكَرَ السُّدِّي: أَنَّهُمْ إِنَّمَا سَجَنُوهُ لِئَلَّا يَشِيعَ مَا كَانَ مِنْهَا فِي حَقِّهِ، وَيَبْرَأَ عِرْضُهُ فَيَفْضَحَهَا.

---

## 12:36 — verse 36

### Translation

Qatadah said: one of the two was the king's cupbearer, and the other was his baker.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: the name of the one in charge of the drink was "Nabwa," and the other was "Majlath."

Al-Suddi said: the reason the king imprisoned the two of them was that he suspected they had conspired together to poison him in his food and drink.

Yusuf, peace be upon him, had become renowned in the prison for generosity, trustworthiness, truthfulness of speech, good bearing, abundance of worship ﷺ, knowledge of dream interpretation, kindness toward the people of the prison, visiting their sick, and fulfilling their rights. When these two young men entered the prison, they became attached to him and loved him with intense love, and they said to him, "By God, we have come to love you with an overflowing love." He said, "May God bless you both. No one has ever loved me but harm came to me because of that love. My paternal aunt loved me, and harm came to me on her account. My father loved me, and I was harmed because of him. The wife of al-Aziz loved me, and likewise harm came." They said, "By God, we cannot help but love you." 

Then the two of them had a dream. The cupbearer saw himself pressing khamr, that is, grapes, and this is confirmed by the reading of Abdullah ibn Mas'ud: "Indeed I see myself pressing grapes." Ibn Abi Hatim narrated this: [chain] from Ibn Mas'ud, that he recited it as "pressing grapes."

Al-Dahhak said regarding His statement, {Indeed I see myself pressing khamr}: meaning grapes. He said: the people of Oman call grapes "khamr."

Ikrimah said: I saw in my dream that I had planted a grapevine, and it grew. Clusters came forth on it, and I pressed them, then gave the king to drink from them. He said: you will remain in prison three days, then you will come out and give him wine to drink.

The other, who was the baker, said: {Indeed I see myself carrying bread upon my head, from which the birds are eating. Inform us of its interpretation, for we see that you are among the doers of good.}

What is well known among the majority is what we have mentioned, that the two of them had a dream and sought its interpretation.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Abdullah, who said: Yusuf's two companions did not see anything at all; rather, they fabricated a dream in order to test him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كَانَ أَحَدُهُمَا سَاقِيَ الْمَلِكِ، وَالْآخَرُ خَبَّازَهُ.

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: كَانَ اسْمُ الَّذِي عَلَى الشَّرَابِ "نَبَوَا"، وَالْآخَرِ "مجلثَ".

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: وَكَانَ سَبَبُ حَبْسِ الْمَلِكِ إِيَّاهُمَا أَنَّهُ تَوَهَّمَ أَنَّهُمَا تَمَالَآ عَلَى سَمِّهِ فِي طَعَامِهِ وَشَرَابِهِ.

وَكَانَ يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، قَدِ اشْتُهِرَ فِي السِّجْنِ بِالْجُودِ وَالْأَمَانَةِ وَصِدْقِ الْحَدِيثِ، وَحُسْنِ السَّمْتِ وَكَثْرَةِ الْعِبَادَةِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلَامُهُ، وَمَعْرِفَةِ التَّعْبِيرِ وَالْإِحْسَانِ إِلَى أهل السجن وعيادة مَرْضَاهُمْ وَالْقِيَامِ بِحُقُوقِهِمْ. وَلَمَّا دَخَلَ هَذَانِ الْفَتَيَانِ إِلَى السِّجْنِ، تَآلَفَا بِهِ وَأَحَبَّاهُ حُبًّا شَدِيدًا، وَقَالَا لَهُ: وَاللَّهِ لَقَدْ أَحْبَبْنَاكَ حُبًّا زَائِدًا. قَالَ بَارَكَ اللَّهُ فِيكُمَا، إِنَّهُ مَا أَحَبَّنِي أَحَدٌ إِلَّا دَخَلَ عَلَيَّ مِنْ مَحَبَّتِهِ ضَرَرٌ، أَحَبَّتْنِي عَمَّتِي فَدَخَلَ عَلَيَّ الضَّرَرُ بِسَبَبِهَا، وَأَحَبَّنِي أَبِي فَأُوذِيتُ بِسَبَبِهِ، وَأَحَبَّتْنِي امْرَأَةُ الْعَزِيزِ فَكَذَلِكَ، فَقَالَا وَاللَّهِ مَا نَسْتَطِيعُ إِلَّا ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ إِنَّهُمَا رَأَيَا مَنَامًا، فَرَأَى السَّاقِي أَنَّهُ يَعْصِرُ خَمْرًا -يَعْنِي عِنَبًا -وَكَذَلِكَ هِيَ فِي قِرَاءَةِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: "إِنِّي أَرَانِي أَعْصِرُ عِنَبًا". وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ سِنَان، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ هَارُونَ، عَنْ شَرِيك، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ، عَنْ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: أَنَّهُ قَرَأَهَا: "أَعْصِرُ عِنَبًا".

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنِّي أَرَانِي أَعْصِرُ خَمْرًا﴾ يَعْنِي: عِنَبًا. قَالَ: وَأَهْلُ عَمَّانَ يسمُّون الْعِنَبَ خَمْرًا.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: رَأَيْتُ فِيمَا يَرَى النَّائِمُ أَنِّي غَرَسْتُ حَبَلة مِنْ عِنَبٍ، فَنَبَتَتْ. فَخَرَجَ فِيهِ عَنَاقِيدُ، فَعَصَرْتُهُنَّ ثُمَّ سَقَيْتُهُنَّ الْمَلِكَ. قَالَ تَمْكُثُ فِي السِّجْنِ ثَلَاثَةَ أَيَّامٍ، ثُمَّ تَخْرُجُ فَتَسْقِيَهُ خَمْرًا.

وَقَالَ الْآخَرُ -وَهُوَ الْخَبَّازُ -: ﴿إِنِّي أَرَانِي أَحْمِلُ فَوْقَ رَأْسِي خُبْزًا تَأْكُلُ الطَّيْرُ مِنْهُ نَبِّئْنَا بِتَأْوِيلِهِ إِنَّا نَرَاكَ مِنَ الْمُحْسِنِينَ﴾

وَالْمَشْهُورُ عِنْدَ الْأَكْثَرِينَ مَا ذَكَرْنَاهُ، وَأَنَّهُمَا رَأَيَا مَنَامًا وَطَلَبَا تَعْبِيرَهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَكِيع وَابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا جَرِيرٌ، عَنْ عُمَارَةَ بْنِ الْقَعْقَاعِ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: مَا رَأَى صَاحِبَا يُوسُفَ شَيْئًا، إِنَّمَا كَانَا تَحَالَمَا لِيُجَرِّبَا عَلَيْهِ.

---

## 12:37-38 — verses 37-38 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Yusuf, peace be upon him, informs the two of them that whatever dream they see in their sleep, he knows its interpretation and will tell them its meaning before it occurs. This is why he said: {No food will come to you as your provision but that I will inform you of its interpretation before it comes to you.}

Mujahid said: he means, {No food will come to you as your provision} [in your sleep] {but that I will inform you of its interpretation before it comes to you}. Al-Suddi said the same.

Ibn Abi Hatim, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [chain] Ibn Abbas said: I do not know, perhaps Yusuf, peace be upon him, used to practice augury (i'tiyaf, divining by omens), for I find in the Book of Allah, when he said to the two men: {No food will come to you as your provision but that I will inform you of its interpretation}, that he meant: when the food came sweet or bitter, he would divine from that at that moment. Then Ibn Abbas said: he was simply taught, and so he taught. This is a gharib (singular) report.

Then he said: This is only from Allah's teaching me, for I have shunned the religion of those who disbelieve in Allah and the Last Day, so they hope for neither reward nor punishment in the return. {And I have followed the religion of my fathers, Ibrahim, Ishaq, and Ya'qub} meaning: I have abandoned the path of disbelief and polytheism, and I have followed the path of these messengers, may Allah's prayers and peace be upon them all. And such is the state of whoever follows the path of guidance, follows the messengers, and turns away from the path of the wrongdoers: Allah guides his heart, teaches him what he did not know, and makes him a leader to be followed in good, and a caller to the path of right guidance.

{It was not for us to associate anything with Allah. That is from the favor of Allah upon us and upon mankind} This is tawhid (the affirmation of Allah's oneness), which is the acknowledgment that there is no god but Him alone, with no partner. {From the favor of Allah upon us} means: He revealed it to us and commanded us with it. {And upon mankind} since He made us callers for them to that. {But most of mankind do not give thanks} meaning: they do not recognize Allah's favor upon them in sending messengers to them. Rather {they exchanged the favor of Allah for disbelief and led their people down to the abode of ruin} [Ibrahim: 28].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] that Ibn Abbas used to treat the grandfather as a father, and would say: By Allah, whoever wishes, we will engage in mutual cursing (li'an) with him at the Hijr, Allah has not mentioned a grandfather or a grandmother. Allah, Exalted is He, said, meaning as a report about Yusuf: {And I have followed the religion of my fathers, Ibrahim, Ishaq, and Ya'qub}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُهُمَا يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَنَّهُمَا مَهْمَا رَأَيَا فِي نَوْمِهِمَا مِنْ حُلْمٍ، فَإِنَّهُ عَارِفٌ بِتَفْسِيرِهِ وَيُخْبِرُهُمَا بِتَأْوِيلِهِ قَبْلَ وُقُوعِهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لَا يَأْتِيكُمَا طَعَامٌ تُرْزَقَانِهِ إِلا نَبَّأْتُكُمَا بِتَأْوِيلِهِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَأْتِيَكُمَا﴾

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَقُولُ: ﴿لَا يَأْتِيكُمَا طَعَامٌ تُرْزَقَانِهِ﴾ [فِي نَوْمِكُمَا] ﴿إِلا نَبَّأْتُكُمَا بِتَأْوِيلِهِ قَبْلَ أَنْ يَأْتِيَكُمَا﴾ وَكَذَا قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ الْعَلَاءِ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ -شَيْخٌ لَهُ -حَدَّثَنَا رِشْدِينُ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ ثَوْبَانَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: مَا أَدْرِي لَعَلَّ يُوسُفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، كَانَ يَعْتَافُ وَهُوَ كَذَلِكَ، لِأَنِّي أَجِدُ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ حِينَ قَالَ لِلرَّجُلَيْنِ: ﴿لَا يَأْتِيكُمَا طَعَامٌ تُرْزَقَانِهِ إِلا نَبَّأْتُكُمَا بِتَأْوِيلِهِ﴾ قَالَ: إِذَا جَاءَ الطَّعَامُ حُلْوًا أَوْ مُرًّا اعْتَافَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ. ثُمَّ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّمَا عُلِّمَ فَعَلَّمَ. وَهَذَا أَثَرٌ غَرِيبٌ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ: وَهَذَا إِنَّمَا هُوَ مِنْ تَعْلِيمِ اللَّهِ إِيَّايَ؛ لِأَنِّي اجْتَنَبْتُ مِلَّةَ الْكَافِرِينَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ، فَلَا يَرْجُونَ ثَوَابًا وَلَا عِقَابًا فِي الْمَعَادِ. ﴿وَاتَّبَعْتُ مِلَّةَ آبَائِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ﴾ يَقُولُ: هَجَرْتُ طَرِيقَ الْكُفْرِ وَالشِّرْكِ، وَسَلَكْتُ طَرِيقَ هَؤُلَاءِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ أَجْمَعِينَ، وَهَكَذَا يَكُونُ حَالُ مِنْ سَلَكَ طَرِيقَ الْهُدَى، وَاتَّبَعَ الْمُرْسَلِينَ، وَأَعْرَضَ عَنْ طَرِيقِ الظَّالِمِينَ فَإِنَّهُ يَهْدِي قَلْبَهُ وَيُعَلِّمُهُ مَا لَمْ يَكُنْ يَعْلَمُهُ، وَيَجْعَلُهُ إِمَامًا يُقْتَدَى بِهِ فِي الْخَيْرِ، وَدَاعِيًا إِلَى سَبِيلِ الرَّشَادِ.

﴿مَا كَانَ لَنَا أَنْ نُشْرِكَ بِاللَّهِ مِنْ شَيْءٍ ذَلِكَ مِنْ فَضْلِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْنَا وَعَلَى النَّاسِ﴾ هَذَا التَّوْحِيدُ -وَهُوَ الْإِقْرَارُ بِأَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، ﴿مِنْ فَضْلِ اللَّهِ عَلَيْنَا﴾ أَيْ: أَوْحَاهُ إِلَيْنَا، وَأَمَرَنَا بِهِ ﴿وَعَلَى النَّاسِ﴾ إِذْ جَعَلَنَا دُعَاةً لَهُمْ إِلَى ذَلِكَ ﴿وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ لَا يَشْكُرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَعْرِفُونَ نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهِمْ بِإِرْسَالِ الرُّسُلِ إِلَيْهِمْ، بَلْ ﴿بَدَّلُوا نِعْمَةَ اللَّهِ كُفْرًا وَأَحَلُّوا قَوْمَهُمْ دَارَ الْبَوَارِ﴾ [إِبْرَاهِيمَ: ٢٨] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَان، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجٌ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ؛ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَجْعَلُ الْجَدَّ أَبًا، وَيَقُولُ: وَاللَّهِ فَمَنْ شَاءَ لَاعَنَّاهُ عِنْدَ الحجْر، مَا ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ جَدًّا وَلَا جَدَّةً، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى -يَعْنِي إِخْبَارًا عَنْ يُوسُفَ: ﴿وَاتَّبَعْتُ مِلَّةَ آبَائِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ﴾

---

## 12:39-40 — verses 39-40 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Then Joseph, peace be upon him, turned to address the two young men, calling them to the worship of God alone, without partner, and to strip away all besides Him of the idols that their people worshipped. He said: {Are scattered lords better, or God the One, the Overpowering?}

That is, He who governs all things by the might of His majesty and the greatness of His dominion.

Then he made clear to them that what they worshipped and called gods was nothing but ignorance on their part, and a naming they had invented of their own accord, which their later generations had received from their forebears, having no support from God. Hence he said: {God has not sent down any authority for it}, meaning: no proof and no evidence.

Then he informed them that judgment, disposal, will, and dominion belong entirely to God, and that He has commanded all His servants to worship none but Him. Then he said: {That is the upright religion}, meaning: this to which I call you, the oneness of God and sincerity of deed for His sake, is the straight religion which God has commanded, and for which He has sent down the proof and the evidence, which He loves and is pleased with. {But most people do not know}, meaning: for this reason most of them are polytheists. {And most people, even if you long for it, are not believers} [Yusuf: 103].

Ibn Jurayj said: Joseph turned them away from the interpretation of the dream to this matter because he knew that it would be harmful to one of the two, so he wished to occupy them with something else so that they would not return to asking him about it. But they did return to it, so he repeated the admonition to them.

There is something to consider in what he said, for Joseph had already promised them at the outset that he would interpret the dream. Rather, he made their asking him, done with reverence and respect, a means and an occasion for calling them to monotheism and submission (Islam), because of what he saw in their natures of readiness to accept good, to turn toward it, and to listen attentively to it. Hence, when he had finished calling them, he proceeded to interpret their dream without any repetition of the request, and he said:

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ثُمَّ إِنَّ يُوسُفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، أَقْبَلَ عَلَى الْفَتَيَيْنِ بِالْمُخَاطَبَةِ، وَالدُّعَاءِ لَهُمَا إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ وَخَلْع مَا سِوَاهُ مِنَ الْأَوْثَانِ الَّتِي يَعْبُدُهَا قَوْمُهُمَا، فَقَالَ: ﴿أَأَرْبَابٌ مُتَفَرِّقُونَ خَيْرٌ أَمِ اللَّهُ الْوَاحِدُ الْقَهَّارُ﴾

[أَيْ] الَّذِي وَلِى كُلَّ شَيْءٍ بِعزّ جَلَالِهِ، وَعَظَمَةِ سُلْطَانِهِ.

ثُمَّ بَيَّنَ لَهُمَا أنَّ الَّتِي يَعْبُدُونَهَا وَيُسَمُّونَهَا آلِهَةً، إِنَّمَا هُوَ جَهْلُ مِنْهُمْ، وَتَسْمِيَةٌ مِنْ تِلْقَاءِ أَنْفُسِهِمْ، تَلَقَّاهَا خَلَفهم عَنْ سَلَفهم، وَلَيْسَ لِذَلِكَ مُسْتَنَدٌ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَا أَنزلَ اللَّهُ بِهَا مِنْ سُلْطَانٍ﴾ أَيْ: حُجَّةٍ وَلَا بُرْهَانٍ.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَهُمْ أَنَّ الْحُكْمَ وَالتَّصَرُّفَ وَالْمَشِيئَةَ وَالْمُلْكَ كلَّه لِلَّهِ، وَقَدْ أَمَرَ عِبَادَهُ قَاطِبَةً أَلَّا يَعْبُدُوا إِلَّا إِيَّاهُ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ذَلِكَ الدِّينُ الْقَيِّمُ أَيْ: هَذَا الَّذِي أَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ تَوحيد اللَّهِ، وَإِخْلَاصِ الْعَمَلِ لَهُ، هُوَ الدِّينُ الْمُسْتَقِيمُ، الَّذِي أَمَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِ وأَنْزَلَ بِهِ الْحُجَّةَ وَالْبُرْهَانَ الَّذِي يُحِبُّهُ وَيَرْضَاهُ، ﴿وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَلِهَذَا كَانَ أَكْثَرُهُمْ مُشْرِكِينَ. ﴿وَمَا أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ وَلَوْ حَرَصْتَ بِمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٠٣] .

وَقَدْ قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: إِنَّمَا عَدَلَ بِهِمْ يُوسُفُ عَنْ تَعْبِيرِ الرُّؤْيَا إِلَى هَذَا، لِأَنَّهُ عَرَف أَنَّهَا ضَارَّةٌ لِأَحَدِهِمَا، فَأَحَبَّ أَنْ يَشْغَلَهُمَا بِغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ، لِئَلَّا يُعَاوِدُوهُ فِيهَا، فَعَاوَدُوهُ، فَأَعَادَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَوْعِظَةَ. 

وَفِي هَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ نَظَرٌ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَدْ وَعَدَهما أَوَّلًا بِتَعْبِيرِهَا وَلَكِنْ جَعَلَ سُؤَالَهُمَا لَهُ عَلَى وَجْهِ التَّعْظِيمِ وَالِاحْتِرَامِ وُصْلة وَسَبَبًا إِلَى دُعَائِهِمَا إِلَى التَّوْحِيدِ وَالْإِسْلَامِ، لِمَا رَأَى فِي سَجِيَّتِهِمَا مِنْ قَبُولِ الْخَيْرِ وَالْإِقْبَالِ عَلَيْهِ، وَالْإِنْصَاتِ إِلَيْهِ، وَلِهَذَا لَمَّا فَرَغَ مِنْ دَعْوَتِهِمَا، شَرَعَ فِي تَعْبِيرِ رُؤْيَاهُمَا، مِنْ غَيْرِ تَكْرَارِ سؤال فقال:

---

## 12:41 — verse 41

### Translation

He says to the two of them: {O my two companions of the prison, as for one of you, he will pour wine for his master}, and this is the one who saw that he was pressing wine, but he did not identify him specifically so that the other one would not grieve. This is why he left it unspecified when he said: {and as for the other, he will be crucified and the birds will eat from his head}, and this in reality was the one who had seen that he was carrying bread upon his head.

Then he informed them both that this matter had already been settled and would inevitably come to pass, because the dream rests upon the leg of a bird as long as it has not been interpreted, but once it is interpreted, it comes to pass.

Al-Thawri said, from Umara ibn al-Qa'qa', from Ibrahim, from Abdullah, who said: when he told them what he told them and informed them, they said, "We did not see anything." So he said: {The matter about which you were inquiring has been decided}.

Muhammad ibn Fudayl also related it from Umara, from Ibrahim, from Alqama, from Ibn Mas'ud, with the same content, and Mujahid, Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, and others interpreted it likewise. The gist of it is that whoever fabricates a dream and then interprets it will be bound by his own interpretation of it, and Allah knows best. It has also come in the hadith related by Imam Ahmad, from Mu'awiya ibn Haydah, from the Prophet ﷺ: "The dream rests upon the leg of a bird as long as it has not been interpreted, but once it is interpreted, it comes to pass."

And in the Musnad of Abu Ya'la, by way of Yazid al-Raqqashi, from Anas, as a raised report (marfu'): "The dream belongs to the first one who interprets it."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يقول لهما: ﴿يَا صَاحِبَيِ السِّجْنِ أَمَّا أَحَدُكُمَا فَيَسْقِي رَبَّهُ خَمْرًا﴾ وَهُوَ الَّذِي رَأَى أَنَّهُ يَعْصِرُ خَمْرًا، وَلَكِنَّهُ لَمْ يعينِّه لِئَلَّا يَحْزَنَ ذَاكَ، وَلِهَذَا أَبْهَمَهُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَأَمَّا الآخَرُ فَيُصْلَبُ فَتَأْكُلُ الطَّيْرُ مِنْ رَأْسِهِ﴾ وَهُوَ فِي نَفْسِ الْأَمْرِ الَّذِي رَأَى أَنَّهُ يَحْمِلُ فَوْقَ رَأْسِهِ خُبْزًا.

ثُمَّ أَعْلَمَهُمَا أَنَّ هَذَا قَدْ فُرغ مِنْهُ، وَهُوَ وَاقِعٌ لَا مَحَالَةَ؛ لِأَنَّ الرُّؤْيَا عَلَى رِجْلِ طَائِرٍ مَا لَمْ تُعَبر، فَإِذَا عُبِّرَت وَقَعت.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ عُمَارَةَ بْنِ الْقَعْقَاعِ عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: لَمَّا قَالَا مَا قَالَا وَأَخْبَرَهُمَا، قَالَا مَا رَأَيْنَا شَيْئًا. فَقَالَ: ﴿قُضِيَ الأمْرُ الَّذِي فِيهِ تَسْتَفْتِيَانِ﴾

وَرَوَاهُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ فُضَيْلٍ عَنْ عُمَارَةَ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ عَلْقَمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ بِهِ، وَكَذَا فَسَّرَهَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ. وَحَاصِلُهُ أَنَّ مَنْ تحلَّم بِبَاطِلٍ وفَسّره، فَإِنَّهُ يُلزَم بِتَأْوِيلِهِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ الَّذِي رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، عَنْ مُعَاوِيَةَ بْنِ حَيْدة، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: "الرُّؤْيَا عَلَى رِجْلِ طَائِرٍ مَا لَمْ تُعَبر فَإِذَا عُبِّرت وَقَعَتْ" 

وَفِي مُسْنَدِ أَبِي يَعْلَى، مِنْ طَرِيقِ يَزِيدَ الرَّقاشي، عَنْ أَنَسٍ مَرْفُوعًا: "الرُّؤْيَا لِأَوَّلِ عَابِرٍ"

---

## 12:42 — verse 42

### Translation

When Yusuf, peace be upon him, judged that one of the two would be saved, that is, the cupbearer, Yusuf said to him privately, apart from the other, and God knows best, so as not to alert him that he was the one to be crucified, he said to him: {Mention me before your master}, meaning: mention my case before your master, that is, the king. But the one entrusted with this forgot to remind his master of it, and this was among the schemes of Satan, so that the prophet of God would not be released from prison.

This is the correct view, that the pronoun in His statement {but Satan caused him to forget the mention of his master} refers to the one who was saved, as Mujahid, Muhammad ibn Ishaq, and others have said. It is also said that the pronoun refers to Yusuf, peace be upon him, as reported by Ibn Jarir from Ibn Abbas, and also from Mujahid, Ikrimah, and others. Ibn Jarir gave a chain here for a hadith, saying:

[chain] Ibn Waki, from Amr ibn Muhammad, from Ibrahim ibn Yazid, from Amr ibn Dinar, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: The Prophet ﷺ said: "Had he not said, meaning Yusuf, the word that he said, he would not have remained in prison as long as he remained, for he sought relief from other than God."

This hadith is very weak, because Sufyan ibn Waki is weak, and Ibrahim ibn Yazid, who is al-Khuzi, is even weaker than him. It has also been reported from al-Hasan and Qatadah as mursal (a report with a missing link at the Companion level) from each of them, and these mursal reports here are not to be accepted, even if the mursal were accepted in other than this context, and God knows best.

As for "bid" (a term denoting an indefinite small number), Mujahid and Qatadah said: it is what is between three and nine. Wahb ibn Munabbih said: Ayyub remained in his affliction for seven years, Yusuf remained in prison for seven years, and the punishment of Bukhtanassar (Nebuchadnezzar) lasted seven years.

Al-Dahhak reported from Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with both of them: "so he remained in prison bida sinin (a few years)," he said: twelve years. Al-Dahhak said: fourteen years.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ظَنَّ يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، نَجَاةَ أحِدهما -وَهُوَ السَّاقِي -قَالَ لَهُ يُوسُفُ خُفْيَةً عَنِ الْآخَرِ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، لِئَلَّا يُشْعِرَهُ أَنَّهُ الْمَصْلُوبُ قَالَ لَهُ: ﴿اذْكُرْنِي عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ﴾ يَقُولُ: اذْكُرْ قِصَّتِي عِنْدَ رَبِّكَ -وَهُوَ الْمَلِكُ -فَنَسِيَ ذَلِكَ الموصَى أَنْ يُذَكِّر مَوْلَاهُ بِذَلِكَ، وَكَانَ مِنْ جُمْلَةِ مَكَايِدِ الشَّيْطَانِ، لِئَلَّا يَطْلَعَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ مِنَ السِّجْنِ.

هَذَا هُوَ الصَّوَابُ أَنَّ الضَّمِيرَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَأَنْسَاهُ الشَّيْطَانُ ذِكْرَ رَبِّهِ﴾ عَائِدٌ عَلَى النَّاجِي، كَمَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ. وَيُقَالُ: إِنَّ الضَّمِيرَ عَائِدٌ عَلَى يُوسُفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ أَيْضًا، وعِكْرِمة، وَغَيْرِهِمْ. وَأَسْنَدَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ هَاهُنَا حَدِيثًا فَقَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرو بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ يَزِيدَ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "لَوْ لَمْ يَقُلْ -يَعْنِي: يُوسُفَ -الْكَلِمَةَ الَّتِي قَالَ: مَا لَبِثَ فِي السِّجْنِ طُولَ مَا لَبِثَ. حَيْثُ يَبْتَغِي الْفَرَجَ مِنْ عِنْدِ غَيْرِ اللَّهِ" .

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ ضَعِيفٌ جِدًّا؛ لِأَنَّ سُفْيَانَ بْنَ وَكِيع ضَعِيفٌ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ -هُوَ الخُوزي -أَضْعَفُ مِنْهُ أَيْضًا. وَقَدْ رُوي عَنِ الْحَسَنِ وَقَتَادَةَ مُرْسَلًا عَنْ كُلٍّ مِنْهُمَا، وَهَذِهِ المرسَلات هَاهُنَا لَا تُقْبَلُ لَوْ قُبِلَ الْمُرْسَلُ مِنْ حَيْثُ هُوَ فِي غَيْرِ هَذَا الْمَوْطِنِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَأَمَّا "الْبِضْعُ"، فَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ وَقَتَادَةُ: هُوَ مَا بَيْنَ الثَّلَاثِ إِلَى التسع. وقال وهب بن مُنَبَّه: مكث أَيُّوبُ فِي الْبَلَاءِ سَبْعًا وَيُوسُفُ فِي السِّجْنِ سَبْعًا، وَعَذَابُ بُخْتُنَصَّرَ سَبْعًا.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا: فَلَبِثَ فِي السِّجْنِ بِضْعَ سِنِينَ قَالَ: ثِنْتَا عَشْرَةَ سَنَةً. وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: أَرْبَعَ عَشَرَةَ سَنَةً.

---

## 12:43-49 — verses 43-49 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This dream from the king of Egypt was among that which Allah, exalted is He, decreed to be a means for Yusuf's, peace be upon him, release from prison, honored and dignified. This was because the king saw this dream, and it alarmed him and he was amazed by it, wondering what its interpretation could be. So he gathered the priests, the diviners, the great men of his kingdom, and his nobles, and related to them what he had seen, and asked them about its interpretation. But they did not know it, and excused themselves to him by saying that these were {jumbled dreams}, that is, a mixture that had produced this vision of his, {and we are not knowledgeable in the interpretation of dreams}, meaning: even if it were a true vision arising from mixed thoughts, we would still have no knowledge of its interpretation, that is, its meaning.

At that point, the one who had been saved from among the two young men who had been in prison with Yusuf remembered him. Satan had caused him to forget what Yusuf had instructed him to do, namely to mention his case to the king. So then he remembered, {after a period}, meaning after some time (some read it as "after forgetfulness," meaning after a lapse of memory), and he said to the king and those gathered for that purpose: {I will inform you of its interpretation}, meaning the interpretation of this dream, {so send me forth}, meaning send me to Yusuf the truthful one, in prison. The meaning of the passage is: so they sent him, and he went and came back. He said: {Yusuf, O truthful one, explain to us} and he related the dream that the king had seen. At that point Yusuf, peace be upon him, gave him its interpretation, without rebuking that young man for having forgotten what he had instructed him to do, and without setting any condition for his own release before doing so. Rather he said: {You shall sow for seven consecutive years}, meaning: fertility and rain will come to you for seven years in succession. He thus interpreted the cows as years, because they plow the land from which crops and produce are cultivated, and these are represented by the green ears of grain.

Then he guided them as to what they should rely upon during those years, saying: {then whatever you harvest, leave it in its ear, except a little of which you eat}, meaning: whatever produce you gather during these seven years of abundance, store it in its ear, so that it will last longer and be less prone to spoiling quickly, except for the amount that you eat, and let that be little by little, without extravagance, so that you may benefit during the seven hard years. These are the seven barren years that will follow these seven consecutive years of abundance, and they are represented by the lean cows that devour the fat ones, because in the years of drought, what was gathered during the years of abundance will be consumed, and these are represented by the dry ears of grain.

He informed them that these barren years would produce nothing, and that whatever they had sown would yield them nothing in return. Hence he said: {which will consume what you have laid up for them, except a little of what you have stored}.

Then, after that widespread and continuous drought, he gave them the glad tiding that it would be followed by {a year in which people will receive abundant rain}, meaning that rain would come to them, the lands would produce abundantly, and people would press what they used to press according to their custom, such as oil and the like, and sugar and the like, until some of them said that this also includes the milking of milk.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah reported from Ibn Abbas regarding {and therein they will press}: "they will milk."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذِهِ الرُّؤْيَا مِنْ مَلك مِصْرَ مِمَّا قَدّر اللَّهُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهَا كَانَتْ سَبَبًا لِخُرُوجِ يوسفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مِنَ السِّجْنِ مُعزَّزًا مُكَرَّمًا، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ المَلك رَأَى هَذِهِ الرُّؤْيَا، فَهَالَتْهُ وتَعجَّب مَنْ أَمْرِهَا، وَمَا يَكُونُ تَفْسِيرُهَا، فَجَمَعَ الْكَهَنَةَ والحُزَاة وَكُبَرَاءَ دَوْلَتِهِ وَأُمَرَاءَهُ وقَصَّ عَلَيْهِمْ مَا رَأَى، وَسَأَلَهُمْ عَنْ تَأْوِيلِهَا، فَلَمْ يَعْرِفُوا ذَلِكَ، وَاعْتَذَرُوا إِلَيْهِ بِأَنَّ هَذِهِ ﴿أَضْغَاثُ أَحْلامٍ﴾ أَيْ: أَخْلَاطٌ اقْتَضَتْ رُؤْيَاكَ هَذِهِ ﴿وَمَا نَحْنُ بِتَأْوِيلِ الأحْلامِ بِعَالِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَوْ كَانَتْ رُؤْيَا صَحِيحَةً مِنْ أَخْلَاطٍ، لَمَا كَانَ لَنَا مَعْرِفَةً بِتَأْوِيلِهَا، وَهُوَ تَعْبِيرُهَا. فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ تَذَكَّرَ ذَلِكَ الَّذِي نَجَا مِنْ ذَيْنِكَ الْفَتَيَيْنِ اللَّذَيْنِ كَانَا فِي السِّجْنِ مَعَ يُوسُفَ، وَكَانَ الشَّيْطَانُ قَدْ أَنْسَاهُ مَا وَصَّاهُ بِهِ يُوسُفُ، مِنْ ذِكْرِ أَمْرِهِ لِلْمَلِكِ، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ تَذَكَّرَ ﴿بَعْدَ أُمَّةٍ﴾ أَيْ: مُدَّةٍ -وَقَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ: "بَعْدَ أَمِةٍ" أَيْ: بَعْدَ نِسْيَانٍ، فَقَالَ لِلْمَلِكِ وَالَّذِينَ جَمَعَهُمْ لِذَلِكَ: ﴿أَنَا أُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِتَأْوِيلِهِ﴾ أَيْ: بِتَأْوِيلِ هَذَا الْمَنَامِ، ﴿فَأَرْسِلُونِ﴾ أَيْ: فَابْعَثُونِ إِلَى يُوسُفَ الصِّدِّيقِ إِلَى السِّجْنِ. وَمَعْنَى الْكَلَامِ: فَبَعَثُوا فَجَاءَ. فَقَالَ: ﴿يُوسُفُ أَيُّهَا الصِّدِّيقُ أَفْتِنَا﴾ وَذَكَرَ الْمَنَامَ الَّذِي رَآهُ الْمَلِكُ، فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ ذَكَرَ لَهُ يُوسُفُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، تَعْبِيرَهَا مِنْ غَيْرِ تَعْنِيفٍ لِذَلِكَ الْفَتَى فِي نِسْيَانِهِ مَا وَصَّاهُ بِهِ، وَمِنْ غَيْرِ اشْتِرَاطٍ لِلْخُرُوجِ قَبْلَ ذَلِكَ، بَلْ قَالَ: ﴿تَزْرَعُونَ سَبْعَ سِنِينَ دَأَبًا﴾ أَيْ يَأْتِيكُمُ الْخِصْبُ وَالْمَطَرُ سَبْعَ سِنِينَ مُتَوَالِيَاتٍ، فَفَسَّرَ الْبَقَرَ بِالسِّنِينَ؛ لِأَنَّهَا تُثِيرُ الْأَرْضَ الَّتِي تُسْتغل منها الثمرات والزروع، وهن السنبلات الْخُضْرُ، ثُمَّ أَرْشَدَهُمْ إِلَى مَا يَعْتَمِدُونَهُ فِي تِلْكَ السِّنِينَ فَقَالَ: ﴿فَمَا حَصَدْتُمْ فَذَرُوهُ فِي سُنْبُلِهِ إِلا قَلِيلا مِمَّا تَأْكُلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مَهْمَا اسْتَغْلَلْتُمْ فِي هَذِهِ السَّبْعِ السِّنِينَ الْخِصْبَ فَاخْزُنُوهُ فِي سُنْبُلِهِ، لِيَكُونَ أَبْقَى لَهُ وَأَبْعَدَ عَنْ إِسْرَاعِ الْفَسَادِ إِلَيْهِ، إِلَّا الْمِقْدَارَ الَّذِي تَأْكُلُونَهُ، وَلْيَكُنْ قَلِيلًا قَلِيلًا لَا تُسْرِفُوا فِيهِ، لِتَنْتَفِعُوا فِي السَّبْعِ الشِّدَادِ، وَهُنَّ السَّبْعُ السِّنِينَ المُحْل الَّتِي تَعْقُبُ هَذِهِ السَّبْعَ مُتَوَالِيَاتٍ، وَهُنَّ الْبَقَرَاتُ الْعِجَافُ اللَّاتِي يَأْكُلْنَ السِّمان؛ لِأَنَّ سِنِيَّ الجَدْب يُؤْكَلُ فِيهَا مَا جَمَعَوه فِي سِنِيِّ الْخِصْبِ، وَهُنَّ السُّنْبُلَاتُ الْيَابِسَاتُ.

وَأَخْبَرَهُمْ أَنَّهُنَّ لَا يُنْبِتْنَ شَيْئًا، وَمَا بَذَرُوهُ فَلَا يَرْجِعُونَ مِنْهُ إِلَى شَيْءٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿يَأْكُلْنَ مَا قَدَّمْتُمْ لَهُنَّ إِلا قَلِيلا مِمَّا تُحْصِنُونَ﴾

ثُمَّ بَشَّرَهُمْ بَعْدَ الجَدْب الْعَامِ الْمُتَوَالِي بِأَنَّهُ يَعْقُبُهُمْ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ ﴿عَامٌ فِيهِ يُغَاثُ النَّاسُ﴾ أَيْ: يَأْتِيهِمُ الْغَيْثُ، وَهُوَ المَطرُ، وتُغل الْبِلَادُ، ويَعصرُ النَّاسُ مَا كَانُوا يَعْصِرُونَ عَلَى عَادَتِهِمْ، مِنْ زَيْتٍ وَنَحْوِهُ، وَسُكَّرٍ وَنَحْوِهُ حَتَّى قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: يَدْخُلُ فِيهِ حَلْبُ اللَّبَنِ أَيْضًا.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ ﴿وَفِيهِ يَعْصِرُونَ﴾ يَحْلِبُونَ.

---

## 12:50-53 — verses 50-53 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted speaks, informing us about the king, when they returned to him with the interpretation of the vision he had seen, an interpretation that amazed and pleased him greatly. He thus recognized Yusuf's excellence, peace be upon him, his knowledge [and his fine insight into the vision], and the goodness of his character, in the presence of his subjects in his land. So he said, {Bring him to me}, meaning: bring him out of the prison and present him. When the messenger came to him with this, Yusuf refused to leave until the king and his subjects had verified the innocence of his position and the purity of his honor from what had been attributed to him regarding the wife of al-Aziz, and that this imprisonment had not been for any just cause, but was rather oppression and wrongdoing. He said: {Return to your lord and ask him: what was the matter with the women who cut their hands? Indeed my Lord is fully aware of their scheming.}

The Sunnah has come with praise for him for this, drawing attention to his excellence, his nobility, the loftiness of his rank and his patience, may the peace and blessings of Allah be upon him. In the Musnad and the two Sahihs, from the hadith of al-Zuhri, from Sa'id and Abu Salamah, from Abu Hurairah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "We have more right to doubt than Ibrahim, when he said, {My Lord, show me how You give life to the dead. He said: Do you not believe? He said: Yes, but so that my heart may be at ease} [al-Baqarah: 260]. And may Allah have mercy on Lut, he indeed sought refuge with a strong support. And had I remained in prison as long as Yusuf remained, I would have responded to the caller."

Imam Ahmad also said: Affan narrated to us, Hammad ibn Salamah narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Amr narrated to us, from Abu Salamah, from Abu Hurairah, from the Prophet ﷺ, regarding His saying: {So ask him: what was the matter with the women who cut their hands? Indeed my Lord is fully aware of their scheming}, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Had it been me, I would have hastened to respond, and I would not have sought an excuse."

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ibn Uyaynah informed us, from Amr ibn Dinar, from Ikrimah, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have indeed marveled at Yusuf's patience and nobility, and may Allah forgive him, when he was asked about the lean and fat cows, and had I been in his place I would not have answered them until I had stipulated that they release me. And I have indeed marveled at Yusuf's patience and nobility, and may Allah forgive him, when the messenger came to him, for had I been in his place I would have rushed to the door, but he wanted to have an excuse for himself." This is a mursal (a report with a broken chain to the Prophet) hadith.

His saying, the Exalted: {He said: What was your affair when you sought to seduce Yusuf?} is an account of the king, when he gathered the women who had cut their hands, in the presence of the wife of al-Aziz. He addressed them all, though he meant the wife of his vizier, who was al-Aziz, saying: {What was your affair}, meaning your situation and your account, {when you sought to seduce Yusuf}, meaning on the day of the banquet? {They said: Far be it from Allah! We know of no evil on his part}, meaning the women answered the king saying: Far be it from Allah that Yusuf should be accused, by Allah we know of no evil on his part. At that point, {The wife of al-Aziz said: Now the truth has become manifest.}

Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, and others said: she says: now the truth has become clear, has appeared, and has emerged.

{I sought to seduce him, and indeed he is among the truthful}, meaning in his statement: {She sought to seduce me}. {That is so that he may know that I did not betray him in his absence}, she says: I have only confessed this against myself so that my husband may know that I did not betray him in the matter itself, and that the greater forbidden act did not occur. I only sought to seduce this young man, an attempt at seduction, but he refused. For this reason I have confessed, so that it may be known that I am innocent. {And that Allah does not guide the scheming of the treacherous. And I do not absolve myself}, the woman says: and I do not absolve myself, for indeed the soul speaks to itself and desires; this is why I sought to seduce him, for it is inclined to evil, {except one whom my Lord has mercy upon}, meaning except one whom Allah the Exalted has protected. {Indeed my Lord is forgiving and merciful.}

This view is the most well known, the most fitting, and the most suitable to the flow of the story and the meanings of the speech. Al-Mawardi related it in his tafsir, and the great imam Abu al-Abbas Ibn Taymiyyah, may Allah have mercy on him, took up its defense and devoted a separate work to it.

It has also been said that this is from the speech of Yusuf, peace be upon him, namely his statement: {That is so that he may know that I did not betray him} regarding his wife, {in his absence}, the two verses, meaning: I only sent the messenger back so that the king would know my innocence and so that al-Aziz would know {that I did not betray him} regarding his wife {in his absence}, {and that Allah does not guide the scheming of the treacherous. And I do not absolve myself, indeed the soul is prone to evil} [the verse]. This is the view which Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim mentioned exclusively, with no other view besides it.

Ibn Jarir said: Abu Kurayb narrated to us, Waki' narrated to us, from Isra'il, from Simak, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: When the king gathered the women and asked them, "Did you seek to seduce Yusuf?" {They said: Far be it from Allah! We know of no evil on his part. The wife of al-Aziz said: Now the truth has become manifest. I sought to seduce him, and indeed he is among the truthful}, Yusuf said: {That is so that he may know that I did not betray him in his absence [and that Allah does not guide the scheming of the treacherous]}. He said: Then Jibril, peace be upon him, said to him: "And not the day you were inclined toward what you were inclined toward." So he said: {And I do not absolve myself, indeed the soul is prone to evil.}

This is likewise what Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Ikrimah, Ibn Abi al-Hudhayl, al-Dahhak, al-Hasan, Qatadah, and al-Suddi said. But the first view is stronger and more apparent, because the whole flow of the speech is from the speech of the wife of al-Aziz in the presence of the king, and Yusuf, peace be upon him, was not present with them; rather, the king had him brought afterward.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنِ الْمَلِكِ لَمَّا رَجَعُوا إِلَيْهِ بِتَعْبِيرِ رُؤْيَاهُ، الَّتِي كَانَ رَآهَا، بِمَا أَعْجَبَهُ وَأَيْنَقَهُ، فَعَرَفَ فَضْلَ يُوسُفَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَعِلْمَهُ [وَحُسْنَ اطِّلَاعِهِ عَلَى رُؤْيَاهُ] وَحُسْنَ أَخْلَاقِهِ عَلَى مَنْ بِبَلَدِهِ مِنْ رَعَايَاهُ، فَقَالَ ﴿ائْتُونِي بِهِ﴾ أَيْ: أَخْرِجُوهُ مِنَ السِّجْنِ وَأَحْضَرُوهُ. فَلَمَّا جَاءَهُ الرَّسُولُ بِذَلِكَ امْتَنَعَ مِنَ الْخُرُوجِ حَتَّى يَتَحَقَّقَ الْمَلِكُ وَرَعَيَّتُهُ بَرَاءَةَ سَاحَتِهِ، وَنَزَاهَةَ عِرْضِهِ، مِمَّا نُسِبَ إِلَيْهِ مِنْ جِهَةِ امْرَأَةِ الْعَزِيزِ، وَأَنَّ هَذَا السِّجْنَ لَمْ يَكُنْ عَلَى أَمْرٍ يَقْتَضِيهِ، بَلْ كَانَ ظُلْمًا وَعُدْوَانًا، قَالَ: ﴿ارْجِعْ إِلَى رَبِّكَ فَاسْأَلْهُ مَا بَالُ النِّسْوَةِ اللاتِي قَطَّعْنَ أَيْدِيَهُنَّ إِنَّ رَبِّي بِكَيْدِهِنَّ عَلِيمٌ﴾

وَقَدْ وَرَدَتِ السَّنَةُ بِمَدْحِهِ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، وَالتَّنْبِيهِ عَلَى فَضْلِهِ وَشَرَفِهِ، وعُلُوّ قَدْرِهِ وَصَبْرِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ الله وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، فَفِي الْمُسْنَدِ وَالصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ وَأَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "نَحْنُ أَحَقُّ بِالشَّكِّ مِنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ إِذْ قَالَ ﴿رَبِّ أَرِنِي كَيْفَ تُحْيِ الْمَوْتَى قَالَ أَوَلَمْ تُؤْمِنْ قَالَ بَلَى وَلَكِنْ لِيَطْمَئِنَّ قَلْبِي﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٦٠] وَيَرْحَمُ اللَّهُ لُوطًا لَقَدْ كَانَ يَأْوِي إِلَى رُكْنٍ شَدِيدٍ، وَلَوْ لَبِثْتُ فِي السِّجْنِ مَا لَبِثَ يُوسُفُ لَأَجَبْتُ الدَّاعِيَ" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَاسْأَلْهُ مَا بَالُ النِّسْوَةِ اللاتِي قَطَّعْنَ أَيْدِيَهُنَّ إِنَّ رَبِّي بِكَيْدِهِنَّ عَلِيمٌ﴾ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لو كُنْتُ أَنَا لَأَسْرَعْتُ الْإِجَابَةَ، وَمَا ابْتَغَيْتُ الْعُذْرَ" .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ عُيَيْنَة، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنْ عِكْرِمة قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَقَدْ عَجِبْتُ مِنْ يُوسُفَ وَصَبْرِهِ وَكَرَمِهِ، وَاللَّهُ يَغْفِرُ لَهُ، حِينَ سُئل عَنِ الْبَقَرَاتِ العِجاف والسِّمان، وَلَوْ كُنْتُ مَكَانَهُ مَا أَجَبْتُهُمْ حَتَّى أَشْتَرِطَ أَنْ يُخْرِجُونِي. وَلَقَدْ عَجِبْتُ مِنْ يُوسُفَ وَصَبْرِهِ وَكَرَمِهِ، وَاللَّهُ يَغْفِرُ لَهُ، حِينَ أَتَاهُ الرَّسُولُ، ولو كنت مكانه لبادرتهم الباب، َ وَلَكِنَّهُ أَرَادَ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ الْعُذْرُ". هَذَا حَدِيثٌ مُرْسَلٌ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قَالَ مَا خَطْبُكُنَّ إِذْ رَاوَدْتُنَّ يُوسُفَ عَنْ نَفْسِهِ﴾ إِخْبَارٌ عَنِ الْمَلِكِ حِينَ جَمَعَ النِّسْوَةَ اللَّاتِي قَطَّعْنَ أَيْدِيَهُنَّ عِنْدَ امْرَأَةِ الْعَزِيزِ، فَقَالَ مُخَاطِبًا لَهُنَّ كُلَّهُنَّ -وَهُوَ يُرِيدُ امْرَأَةَ وَزِيرِهِ، وَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ -: ﴿مَا خَطْبُكُنَّ﴾ أَيْ: شَأْنُكُنَّ وَخَبَرُكُنَّ ﴿إِذْ رَاوَدْتُنَّ يُوسُفَ عَنْ نَفْسِهِ﴾ يَعْنِي: يَوْمَ الضِّيَافَةِ؟ ﴿قُلْنَ حَاشَ لِلَّهِ مَا عَلِمْنَا عَلَيْهِ مِنْ سُوءٍ﴾ أَيْ: قَالَتِ النِّسْوَةُ جَوَابًا لِلْمَلِكِ: حَاشَ لِلَّهِ أَنْ يَكُونَ يُوسُفَ مُتَّهَمَا، وَاللَّهِ مَا عَلِمْنَا عَلَيْهِ مِنْ سُوءٍ. فَعِنْدَ ذَلِكَ ﴿قَالَتِ امْرَأَةُ الْعَزِيزِ الآنَ حَصْحَصَ الْحَقُّ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: تَقُولُ الْآنَ: تَبَيَّنَ الْحَقُّ وَظَهَرَ وَبَرَزَ.

﴿أَنَا رَاوَدْتُهُ عَنْ نَفْسِهِ وَإِنَّهُ لَمِنَ الصَّادِقِينَ﴾ أَيْ: فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿هِيَ رَاوَدَتْنِي عَنْ نَفْسِي﴾ ﴿ذَلِكَ لِيَعْلَمَ أَنِّي لَمْ أَخُنْهُ بِالْغَيْبِ﴾ تَقُولُ: إِنَّمَا اعْتَرَفْتُ بِهَذَا عَلَى نَفْسِي، ذَلِكَ لِيَعْلَمَ زَوْجِي أَنْ لَمْ أَخُنْهُ فِي نَفْسِ الْأَمْرِ، وَلَا وَقَعَ الْمَحْذُورُ الْأَكْبَرُ، وَإِنَّمَا رَاوَدْتُ هَذَا الشَّابَّ مُرَاوَدَةً، فَامْتَنَعَ؛ فَلِهَذَا اعترفتُ لِيَعْلَمَ أَنِّي بَرِيئَةٌ، ﴿وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَهْدِي كَيْدَ الْخَائِنِينَ وَمَا أُبَرِّئُ نَفْسِي﴾ تَقُولُ الْمَرْأَةُ: وَلَسْتُ أُبَرِّئُ نَفْسِي، فَإِنَّ النَّفْسَ تَتَحَدَّثُ وَتَتَمَنَّى؛ وَلِهَذَا رَاوَدَتْهُ لِأَنَّهَا أَمَارَةٌ بِالسُّوءِ، ﴿إِلا مَا رَحِمَ رَبِّي﴾ أَيْ: إِلَّا مَنْ عَصَمَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، ﴿إِنَّ رَبِّي غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾ .
