The Almighty informs us that His help descends upon His messengers, God's prayers and peace be upon all of them, at the time of hardship and while awaiting relief from God in the moments of greatest need for it, as in His statement: {And they were shaken until the Messenger and those who believed with him said, "When is the help of God?" Unquestionably, the help of God is near} [al-Baqarah: 214]. Regarding His statement {kudhibu}, there are two readings. One of them, with the doubled letter, is "qad kudhdhibu" (they were denied/rejected), and this is how Aisha, may God be pleased with her, used to recite it. Al-Bukhari said:

[chain] Urwah ibn al-Zubayr reported that Aisha, when he asked her about God's statement {until when the messengers despaired}, said to him: I said, "Was it 'ukdhibu' or 'kudhdhibu'?" Aisha said: "Kudhdhibu" (they were denied). I said: "But they were already certain that their people had denied them, so how could it be mere assumption?" She said: "Indeed, by my life, they were certain of that." I said to her: "And did they think that they themselves had been given false promises?" She said: "God forbid! The messengers would never think that of their Lord." I said: "Then what does this verse mean?" She said: "They are the followers of the messengers who believed in their Lord and confirmed them as true. The trial grew long upon them and help was delayed from them, {until when the messengers despaired} of those among their people who had denied them, and the messengers thought that their followers had denied them, God's help came to them at that point."

[chain] Abu al-Yaman narrated to us, Shu'ayb informed us, from al-Zuhri who said: Urwah informed us, and I said: "Perhaps it is 'qad kudhibu' with the light letter?" She said: "God forbid!" This is the end of what he mentioned.

Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abi Mulaykah informed me that Ibn Abbas recited it {wa zannu annahum qad kudhibu} with the light letter. Abd Allah, that is Ibn Mulaykah, said: Then Ibn Abbas said to me: "They were human beings," and Ibn Abbas recited {until the Messenger and those who believed with him said, 'When is the help of God?' Unquestionably, the help of God is near} [al-Baqarah: 214]. Ibn Jurayj said: Ibn Abi Mulaykah said to me: Urwah informed me, from Aisha, that she opposed this and rejected it, and said: "God never promised Muhammad ﷺ anything except that he knew it would come to pass, until he died. Rather, the trial continued upon the messengers until they thought that those believers who were with them had denied them." Ibn Abi Mulaykah said in the report of Urwah: Aisha used to recite it {wa zannu annahum qad kudhdhibu}, with the doubled letter, meaning denial (takdhib).

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Yahya ibn Sa'id said: A man came to al-Qasim ibn Muhammad and said: "Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi says this verse is {until when the messengers despaired and thought that they had been kudhibu}." Al-Qasim said: "Tell him from me that I heard Aisha, the wife of the Prophet ﷺ, say: {until when the messengers despaired and thought that they had been kudhibu}, meaning: their followers denied them." This chain is also sound.

The second reading, with the light letter, and they differed regarding its interpretation. Ibn Abbas said what was mentioned above. And from Ibn Mas'ud, as reported by Sufyan al-Thawri, from al-A'mash, from Abu al-Duha, from Masruq, from Abd Allah, that he recited {until when the messengers despaired and thought that they had been kudhibu} with the light letter. Abd Allah said: "This is the reading that you dislike."

This report from Ibn Mas'ud and Ibn Abbas, may God be pleased with them both, conflicts with what others reported from them. As for Ibn Abbas, al-A'mash reported from Muslim, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His statement {until when the messengers despaired and thought that they had been kudhibu}, that he said: "When the messengers despaired that their people would respond to them, and their people thought that the messengers had lied to them (kadhdhabuhum), help came to them at that point, {and We saved whom We willed}."

The same was reported from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Imran ibn al-Harith al-Sulami, Abd al-Rahman ibn Mu'awiyah, Ali ibn Abi Talhah, and al-'Awfi from Ibn Abbas, similarly.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibrahim ibn Abi Hurrah al-Jazari said: A young man from Quraysh asked Sa'id ibn Jubayr, saying: "O Abu Abd Allah, how is this word? For whenever I come upon it I wish I had not recited this surah: {until when the messengers despaired and thought that they had been kudhibu}?" He said: "Yes, until when the messengers despaired of their people believing them, and those to whom the messengers were sent thought that the messengers had lied (kadhabu) to them." Then al-Dahhak ibn Muzahim said: "I have never seen the like of this day, a man being called to knowledge and hesitating! Had I traveled to Yemen for this it would have been little."

Then Ibn Jarir also reported by another route that Muslim ibn Yasar asked Sa'id ibn Jubayr about this, and he gave him this same answer, whereupon he rose to Sa'id and embraced him, saying: "May God relieve you as you have relieved me."

Thus it has been reported through more than one route from Sa'id ibn Jubayr that he interpreted it in this way, and likewise Mujahid ibn Jabr and more than one of the early generations interpreted it, to the point that Mujahid recited it as "wa zannu annahum qad kadhabu" with the fatha on the dhal. Ibn Jarir reported this, except that some of those who interpreted it this way return the pronoun in His statement {wa zannu annahum qad kudhibu} to the believing followers of the messengers, while others return it to the disbelievers among them, meaning: the disbelievers thought that the messengers had lied (kadhabu), with the light letter, regarding what they had promised of help.

As for Ibn Mas'ud, Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Tamim ibn Hadhlam said: I heard Abd Allah ibn Mas'ud say regarding this verse: {until when the messengers despaired} of their people believing in them, and their people, when the matter was delayed, thought that they (the messengers) had lied (kadhabu), with the light letter.

These are the two reports from each of Ibn Mas'ud and Ibn Abbas. Aisha rejected this interpretation from those who interpreted it thus, and Ibn Jarir supported her view, explaining the well known position held by the majority, and thoroughly discredited the other view, rejecting it and refusing it, neither accepting it nor approving of it. And God knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّ نَصْرَهُ يَنْزِلُ عَلَى رُسُلِهِ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ أَجْمَعِينَ، عِنْدَ ضَيِّقِ الْحَالِ وَانْتِظَارِ الْفَرَجِ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى فِي أَحْوَجِ الْأَوْقَاتِ إِلَى ذَلِكَ، كَمَا فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَزُلْزِلُوا حَتَّى يَقُولَ الرَّسُولُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ مَتَى نَصْرُ اللَّهِ أَلا إِنَّ نَصْرَ اللَّهِ قَرِيبٌ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢١٤] ، وَفِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿كُذِبُوا﴾ قِرَاءَتَانِ، إِحْدَاهُمَا بِالتَّشْدِيدِ: "قَدْ كُذِّبُوا"، وَكَذَلِكَ كَانَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا، تَقْرَؤُهَا، قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْعَزِيزِ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، حَدَّثَنَا إبراهيم بن سعد، بن صالح، عن ابن شهاب قال: أَخْبَرَنِي عُرْوَةُ بْنُ الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ لَهُ وَهُوَ يَسْأَلُهَا عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْئَسَ الرُّسُلُ﴾ قَالَ: قُلْتُ: أكُذِبوا أَمْ كُذِّبوا؟ فَقَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: كُذِّبوا. فَقُلْتُ: فَقَدِ اسْتَيْقَنُوا أَنَّ قَوْمَهُمْ قَدْ كَذَّبوهم فَمَا هُوَ بِالظَّنِّ؟ قَالَتْ: أَجَلْ، لَعَمْرِي لَقَدِ اسْتَيْقَنُوا بِذَلِكَ. فَقُلْتُ لَهَا: وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِّبُوا؟ قَالَتْ مَعَاذَ اللَّهِ، لَمْ تَكُنِ الرُّسُلُ تَظُنُّ ذَلِكَ بِرَبِّهَا. قُلْتُ: فَمَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ؟ قَالَتْ: هُمْ أَتْبَاعُ الرُّسُلِ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِرَبِّهِمْ وَصَدَّقُوهُمْ، فَطَالَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْبَلَاءُ، وَاسْتَأْخَرَ عَنْهُمُ النَّصْرُ، ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْئَسَ الرُّسُلُ﴾ مِمَّنْ كَذَّبَهُمْ مِنْ قَوْمِهِمْ، وَظَنَّتِ الرُّسُلُ أَنَّ أَتْبَاعَهُمْ قَدْ كذَّبوهم، جَاءَهُمْ نَصْرُ اللَّهِ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ.

حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْيَمَانِ، أَنْبَأَنَا شُعَيْبٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ قَالَ: أَخْبَرَنَا عُرْوَة، فَقُلْتُ: لَعَلَّهَا قَدْ كُذِبوا مُخَفَّفَةً؟ قَالَتْ: مَعَاذَ اللَّهِ. انْتَهَى مَا ذَكَرَهُ. 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج أَخْبَرَنِي ابْنُ أَبَى مُلَيْكة: أَنَّ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ قَرَأَهَا: ﴿وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِبُوا﴾ خَفِيفَةً -قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ هُوَ ابْنُ مُلَيْكة: ثُمَّ قَالَ لِي ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانُوا بَشَرًا وَتَلَا ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿حَتَّى يَقُولَ الرَّسُولُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ مَتَى نَصْرُ اللَّهِ أَلا إِنَّ نَصْرَ اللَّهِ قَرِيبٌ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢١٤] ، قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: وَقَالَ لِي ابْنُ أَبِي مُلَيْكَةَ: وَأَخْبَرَنِي عُرْوَةُ عَنْ عَائِشَةَ: أَنَّهَا خَالَفَتْ ذَلِكَ وَأَبَتْهُ، وَقَالَتْ: مَا وَعَدَ اللَّهُ مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ مِنْ شَيْءٍ إِلَّا قَدْ عَلِمَ أَنَّهُ سَيَكُونُ حَتَّى مَاتَ، وَلَكِنَّهُ لَمْ يَزَلِ الْبَلَاءُ بِالرُّسُلِ حَتَّى ظَنُّوا أنَّ مَنْ مَعَهُمْ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ قَدْ كذَّبوهم. قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي مُلَيْكَةَ فِي حَدِيثِ عُرْوَةَ: كَانَتْ عَائِشَةُ تَقْرَؤُهَا "وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِّبوا" مُثْقَلَةً، لِلتَّكْذِيبِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: أَنَا يُونُسُ بْنُ عَبَدِ الْأَعْلَى قِرَاءَةً، أَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ بِلَالٍ، عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ إِنْسَانٌ إِلَى الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ مُحَمَّدَ بْنَ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيَّ يَقُولُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْئَسَ الرُّسُلُ وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِبُوا﴾ فَقَالَ الْقَاسِمُ: أَخْبِرْهُ عَنِّي أَنِّي سَمِعْتُ عَائِشَةَ زَوْجَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ تَقُولُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيأَسَ الرُّسُلُ وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِبُوا﴾ تَقُولُ: كَذَّبَتْهُمْ أَتْبَاعُهُمْ. إِسْنَادٌ صَحِيحٌ أَيْضًا.

وَالْقِرَاءَةُ الثَّانِيَةُ بِالتَّخْفِيفِ، وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي تَفْسِيرِهَا، فَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ مَا تَقَدَّمَ، وَعَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، فِيمَا رَوَاهُ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي الضُّحى، عَنْ مَسْرُوقٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ أَنَّهُ قَرَأَ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْأَسَ الرُّسُلُ وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِبُوا﴾ مُخَفَّفَةً، قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ: هُوَ الَّذِي تَكْرَهُ. 

وَهَذَا عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، مُخَالِفٌ لِمَا رَوَاهُ آخَرُونَ عَنْهُمَا. أَمَّا ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ فَرَوَى الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْأَسَ الرُّسُلُ وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِبُوا﴾ قَالَ: لَمَّا أَيِسَتِ الرُّسُلُ أَنْ يَسْتَجِيبَ لَهُمْ قَوْمُهُمْ، وظن قومهم أن الرسل قد كَذَّبوهم، جَاءَهُمُ النَّصْرُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، ﴿فَنُجِّيَ مَنْ نَشَاءُ﴾ 

وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَعِمْرَانَ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ السُّلَمِيِّ، وَعَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ مُعَاوِيَةَ وعلي بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، وَالْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ بِمِثْلِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْمُثَنَّى، حَدَّثَنَا عَارِمٌ أَبُو النُّعْمَانِ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعَيْبٌ حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ أَبِي حُرة الجزرِيّ قَالَ: سَأَلَ فَتَى مِنْ قُرَيْشٍ سَعِيدَ بْنَ جُبَيْرٍ فَقَالَ لَهُ: يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ هَذَا الْحَرْفُ، فَإِنِّي إِذَا أَتَيْتُ عَلَيْهِ تَمَنَّيْتُ أَنِّي لَا أَقْرَأُ هَذِهِ السُّورَةَ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيأَسَ الرُّسُلُ وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِبُوا﴾ ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ، حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْأَسَ الرُّسُلُ مِنْ قَوْمِهِمْ أَنْ يصدِّقوهم، وَظَنَّ المرسَلُ إِلَيْهِمْ أَنَّ الرُّسُلَ كَذَبوا. فَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ بْنُ مزاحم: ما رأيت كاليوم قط رجل يُدْعَى إِلَى عِلْمٍ فَيَتَلَكَّأُ! لَوْ رَحَلْتُ فِي هَذِهِ إِلَى الْيَمَنِ كَانَ قَلِيلًا.

ثُمَّ رَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ: أَنَّ مُسْلِمَ بْنَ يَسَار سَأَلَ سَعِيدَ بْنَ جُبَيْرٍ عَنْ ذَلِكَ، فَأَجَابَهُ بِهَذَا الْجَوَابِ، فَقَامَ إِلَى سَعِيدٍ فَاعْتَنَقَهُ، وَقَالَ: فرَّج اللَّهُ عَنْكَ كَمَا فَرجت عَنِّي.

وَهَكَذَا رُوِيَ مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ أَنَّهُ فَسَّرَهَا كَذَلِكَ، وَكَذَا فَسَّرَهَا مُجَاهِدُ بْنُ جَبْر، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ، حَتَّى إِنَّ مُجَاهِدًا قَرَأَهَا: "وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كَذَبوا"، بِفَتْحِ الذَّالِ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، إِلَّا أَنَّ بَعْضَ مَنْ فَسَّرَهَا كَذَلِكَ يُعِيدُ الضَّمِيرَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَظَنُّوا أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كُذِبُوا﴾ إِلَى أَتْبَاعِ الرُّسُلِ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يُعِيدُهُ إِلَى الْكَافِرِينَ مِنْهُمْ، أَيْ: وَظَنَّ الْكُفَّارُ أَنَّ الرُّسُلَ قَدْ كَذبوا -مُخَفَّفَةً -فِيمَا وَعَدُوا بِهِ مِنَ النَّصْرِ.

وَأَمَّا ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ فَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا الْقَاسِمُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحُسَيْنُ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ فُضَيْلٍ عَنْ جَحش بْنِ زِيَادٍ الضَّبِّيِّ، عَنْ تَمِيمِ بْنِ حَذْلَم قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ مَسْعُودٍ يَقُولُ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا اسْتَيْأَسَ الرُّسُلُ﴾ مِنْ إِيمَانِ قَوْمِهِمْ أَنْ يُؤْمِنُوا بِهِمْ وَظَنَّ قَوْمُهُمْ حِينَ أَبْطَأَ الْأَمْرُ أَنَّهُمْ قَدْ كَذَبوا، بِالتَّخْفِيفِ. 

فَهَاتَانِ الرِّوَايَتَانِ عَنْ كُلٍّ مِنَ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ وَابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَقَدْ أَنْكَرَتْ ذَلِكَ عَائِشَةُ عَلَى مَنْ فَسَّرَهَا بِذَلِكَ، وَانْتَصَرَ لَهَا ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَوَجَّهَ الْمَشْهُورَ عَنِ الْجُمْهُورِ، وَزَيَّفَ الْقَوْلَ الْآخَرَ بِالْكُلِّيَّةِ، وردَّهُ وأبَاه، وَلَمْ يَقْبَلْهُ وَلَا ارْتَضَاهُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 12:111 — verse 111

### Translation

The Almighty says: In the account of the messengers with their peoples, and how We saved the believers and destroyed the disbelievers, there is {a lesson for the possessors of understanding}, that is, sound minds. {It is not a narration that has been invented}, meaning: it was not possible for this Qur'an to be fabricated apart from God, that is, to be falsified and made up. {But it is a confirmation of what came before it}, meaning: of the books sent down from heaven, for it confirms what is sound within them and negates what occurred in them of distortion, alteration, and change, and it passes judgment upon them either by abrogation or by affirmation. {And a detailed explanation of everything}, of what is permitted and what is forbidden, of what is loved and what is disliked, and other matters such as commands to obedience, to obligatory and recommended acts, and prohibitions of forbidden things and similar disliked matters, and reports about matters as they clearly are, and about future unseen things both in general and in detail, and reports about the Lord, Blessed and Exalted, concerning His names and attributes, and His transcendence above any resemblance to created things. For this reason it was {guidance and mercy for a people who believe}, their hearts being guided by it from error to right guidance, and from misguidance to correctness, and they seek through it the mercy of the Lord of servants, in this worldly life and on the Day of Return.

We ask God, the Magnificent, to make us among them in this world and the next, on the Day when those whose faces are made radiantly white will triumph with the gain, while those whose faces are blackened will return with the losing bargain.

This is the end of the tafsir of Surat Yusuf. Praise and grace belong to God, and in Him is help sought and upon Him is reliance placed, and He is sufficient for us and the best of guardians.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: لَقَدْ كَانَ فِي خَبَرِ الْمُرْسَلِينَ مَعَ قَوْمِهِمْ، وَكَيْفَ أَنْجَيْنَا الْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَأَهْلَكْنَا الْكَافِرِينَ ﴿عِبْرَةٌ لأولِي الألْبَابِ﴾ وَهِيَ الْعُقُولُ، ﴿مَا كَانَ حَدِيثًا يُفْتَرَى﴾ أَيْ: وَمَا كَانَ لِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ أَنْ يُفْتَرَى مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، أَيْ: يُكَذَّبَ ويُختلق، ﴿وَلَكِنْ تَصْدِيقَ الَّذِي بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْكُتُبِ الْمُنَزَّلَةِ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ، وَهُوَ يُصَدِّقُ مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الصَّحِيحِ، وَيَنْفِي مَا وَقَعَ فِيهَا مِنْ تَحْرِيفٍ وَتَبْدِيلٍ وَتَغْيِيرٍ، وَيَحْكُمُ عَلَيْهَا بِالنَّسَخِ أَوِ التَّقْرِيرِ، ﴿وَتَفْصِيلَ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ﴾ مِنْ تَحْلِيلٍ وَتَحْرِيمٍ، وَمَحْبُوبٍ وَمَكْرُوهٍ، وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ مِنَ الْأَمْرِ بِالطَّاعَاتِ وَالْوَاجِبَاتِ وَالْمُسْتَحَبَّاتِ، وَالنَّهْيِ عَنِ الْمُحَرَّمَاتِ وَمَا شَاكَلَهَا مِنَ الْمَكْرُوهَاتِ، وَالْإِخْبَارِ عَنِ الْأُمُورِ عَلَى الْجَلِيَّةِ، وَعَنِ الْغُيُوبِ الْمُسْتَقْبَلَةِ الْمُجْمَلَةِ وَالتَّفْصِيلِيَّةِ، وَالْإِخْبَارِ عَنِ الرَّبِّ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى بِالْأَسْمَاءِ وَالصِّفَاتِ، وَتَنْزِيهِهِ عَنْ مُمَاثَلَةِ الْمَخْلُوقَاتِ، فَلِهَذَا كَانَ: ﴿هُدًى وَرَحْمَةً لِقَوْمٍ يُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ تَهْتَدِي بِهِ قُلُوبُهُمْ مِنَ الْغَيِّ إِلَى الرَّشَادِ، وَمِنَ الضَّلَالَةِ إِلَى السَّدَادِ، وَيَبْتَغُونَ بِهِ الرَّحْمَةَ مِنْ رَبِّ الْعِبَادِ، فِي هَذِهِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَيَوْمَ الْمَعَادِ. فَنَسْأَلُ اللَّهَ الْعَظِيمَ أَنْ يَجْعَلَنَا مِنْهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، يَوْمَ يَفُوزُ بِالرِّبْحِ المُبْيَضَّة وُجُوهُهُمُ النَّاضِرَةُ، وَيَرْجِعُ المسودَّة وجوهُهم بِالصَّفْقَةِ الْخَاسِرَةِ.

آخَرُ تَفْسِيرِ سُورَةِ يُوسُفَ، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ وَبِهِ الْمُسْتَعَانُ وَعَلَيْهِ التكلان، وهو حسبنا ونعم الوكيل.

---
